        <div class="stack-line sl-v1"></div>

        <div class="stack-node sn4">NeuralEdge</div>

      <div class="sr d2">
        <div class="stack-code">
          <div class="dots"><i></i><i></i><i></i></div>
          <pre>
<span class="cm">// AI sentiment API in NC</span>
<span class="kw">service</span> <span class="fn">SentimentAPI</span> {

  <span class="kw">route</span> <span class="st">"/analyze"</span> {
    <span class="kw">input</span>  text: <span class="fn">string</span>
    <span class="kw">ai</span>    model: <span class="st">"gpt-4"</span>
    <span class="kw">prompt</span> <span class="st">"Analyze sentiment: {text}"</span>
    <span class="kw">output</span> json
  }

  <span class="kw">deploy</span> port: <span class="nu">3000</span>
}</pre>
        </div>
        <div class="stack-info">
          <h3>Why NC?</h3>
          <ul class="stack-features">
            <li>Plain English syntax — no semicolons, no brackets hell</li>
            <li>AI-native primitives built into the language core</li>
            <li>Single binary output, zero runtime dependencies</li>
            <li>570KB compiler — smaller than most npm packages</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

<script>
(function(){
  'use strict';

  // ── Nav shrink on scroll ──
  const nav = document.getElementById('nav');
  let lastScroll = 0;
  function onScroll(){
    const y = window.scrollY;
    nav.classList.toggle('scrolled', y > 40);
    lastScroll = y;
  }
  window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, {passive:true});

  // ── Hero mouse glow ──
  const hero = document.getElementById('hero');
  const glow = document.getElementById('heroGlow');
  hero.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e){
    const r = hero.getBoundingClientRect();
    glow.style.left = (e.clientX - r.left) + 'px';
    glow.style.top = (e.clientY - r.top) + 'px';
    glow.style.opacity = '1';
  });
  hero.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(){
    glow.style.opacity = '0';
  });

  // ── Scroll reveal (IntersectionObserver) ──
  const srEls = document.querySelectorAll('.sr');
  const srObs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      if(e.isIntersecting){
        e.target.classList.add('vis');
        srObs.unobserve(e.target);
      }
    });
  }, {threshold:0.15, rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});
  srEls.forEach(function(el){ srObs.observe(el); });

  // ── Animated counters ──
  const counters = document.querySelectorAll('.counter');
  const ctrObs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      if(!e.isIntersecting) return;
      const el = e.target;
      const target = parseInt(el.dataset.target, 10);
      if(target === 0){ el.textContent = '0'; ctrObs.unobserve(el); return; }
      const duration = 1800;
      const start = performance.now();
      function tick(now){
        const p = Math.min((now - start) / duration, 1);
        const ease = 1 - Math.pow(1 - p, 3);
        el.textContent = Math.round(target * ease);
        if(p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }
      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      ctrObs.unobserve(el);
    });
  }, {threshold:0.5});
  counters.forEach(function(c){ ctrObs.observe(c); });

  // ── 3D tilt on product cards ──
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-tilt]').forEach(function(card){
    card.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e){
      const r = card.getBoundingClientRect();
      const x = (e.clientX - r.left) / r.width;
      const y = (e.clientY - r.top) / r.height;
      const tiltX = (y - 0.5) * -12;
      const tiltY = (x - 0.5) * 12;
      card.style.transform = 'perspective(800px) rotateX('+tiltX+'deg) rotateY('+tiltY+'deg) scale3d(1.02,1.02,1.02)';
      // Move glow
      const g = card.querySelector('.p-card-glow');
      if(g){
        g.style.left = (e.clientX - r.left - 100) + 'px';
        g.style.top = (e.clientY - r.top - 100) + 'px';
      }
    });
    card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(){
      card.style.transform = 'perspective(800px) rotateX(0) rotateY(0) scale3d(1,1,1)';
      card.style.transition = 'transform .5s cubic-bezier(.4,0,.2,1), box-shadow .4s';
    });
    card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(){
      card.style.transition = 'box-shadow .4s';
    });
  });

  // ── Close mobile nav on link click ──
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links a').forEach(function(a){
    a.addEventListener('click', function(){
      document.querySelector('.nav-links').classList.remove('open');
    });
  });

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<span class="cm">// AI sentiment API in NC</span>
<span class="kw">service</span> <span class="fn">SentimentAPI</span> {

  <span class="kw">route</span> <span class="st">"/analyze"</span> {
    <span class="kw">input</span>  text: <span class="fn">string</span>
    <span class="kw">ai</span>    model: <span class="st">"gpt-4"</span>
    <span class="kw">prompt</span> <span class="st">"Analyze sentiment: {text}"</span>

  }

}</pre>

            <li>Single binary output, zero runtime dependencies</li>

<script>
(function(){
  'use strict';

  // ── Nav shrink on scroll ──
  const nav = document.getElementById('nav');
  let lastScroll = 0;
  function onScroll(){
    const y = window.scrollY;
    nav.classList.toggle('scrolled', y > 40);
    lastScroll = y;
  }
  window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, {passive:true});

  // ── Hero mouse glow ──
  const hero = document.getElementById('hero');
  const glow = document.getElementById('heroGlow');
  hero.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e){
    const r = hero.getBoundingClientRect();
    glow.style.left = (e.clientX - r.left) + 'px';
    glow.style.top = (e.clientY - r.top) + 'px';
    glow.style.opacity = '1';
  });
  hero.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(){
    glow.style.opacity = '0';
  });

  // ── Scroll reveal (IntersectionObserver) ──
  const srEls = document.querySelectorAll('.sr');
  const srObs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      if(e.isIntersecting){
        e.target.classList.add('vis');
        srObs.unobserve(e.target);
      }
    });
  }, {threshold:0.15, rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});
  srEls.forEach(function(el){ srObs.observe(el); });

  // ── Animated counters ──
  const counters = document.querySelectorAll('.counter');
  const ctrObs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      if(!e.isIntersecting) return;
      const el = e.target;
      const target = parseInt(el.dataset.target, 10);
      if(target === 0){ el.textContent = '0'; ctrObs.unobserve(el); return; }
      const duration = 1800;
      const start = performance.now();
      function tick(now){
        const p = Math.min((now - start) / duration, 1);
        const ease = 1 - Math.pow(1 - p, 3);
        el.textContent = Math.round(target * ease);
        if(p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }
      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      ctrObs.unobserve(el);
    });
  }, {threshold:0.5});
  counters.forEach(function(c){ ctrObs.observe(c); });

  // ── 3D tilt on product cards ──
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-tilt]').forEach(function(card){
    card.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e){
      const r = card.getBoundingClientRect();
      const x = (e.clientX - r.left) / r.width;
      const y = (e.clientY - r.top) / r.height;
      const tiltX = (y - 0.5) * -12;
      const tiltY = (x - 0.5) * 12;
      card.style.transform = 'perspective(800px) rotateX('+tiltX+'deg) rotateY('+tiltY+'deg) scale3d(1.02,1.02,1.02)';
      // Move glow
      const g = card.querySelector('.p-card-glow');
      if(g){
        g.style.left = (e.clientX - r.left - 100) + 'px';
        g.style.top = (e.clientY - r.top - 100) + 'px';
      }
    });
    card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(){
      card.style.transform = 'perspective(800px) rotateX(0) rotateY(0) scale3d(1,1,1)';
      card.style.transition = 'transform .5s cubic-bezier(.4,0,.2,1), box-shadow .4s';
    });
    card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(){
      card.style.transition = 'box-shadow .4s';
    });
  });

  // ── Close mobile nav on link click ──
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links a').forEach(function(a){
    a.addEventListener('click', function(){
      document.querySelector('.nav-links').classList.remove('open');
    });
  });

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

    <div class="box box-step" style="border-color:#22c55e"><span class="num" style="background:#22c55e">4</span> GENERATE FIX (ABC)<small>Scout→Worker→Evaluator • Optimal fix selected</small></div>

    <div class="box box-step"><span class="num">5</span> VALIDATE<small>Sandbox dry-run • Side effects checked</small></div>

<!-- ══════════════ WHY IT'S AN "OS" ══════════════ -->
<section id="why-os">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">The Name</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">Why Is It Called an "Operating System"?</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">A traditional OS manages hardware processes, memory, and I/O. HiveANT does the same &mdash; for your entire software infrastructure. It's the operating system layer between your AI agents and your production environment.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="os-grid">
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-kernel">&#x2699;</div>
        <h3>Kernel &amp; Agent Runtime</h3>
        <p>Like a process scheduler in Linux, the HiveANT kernel manages agent lifecycle &mdash; spawning, scheduling, killing, and resource allocation for thousands of concurrent agents.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-sched">&#x23F1;</div>
        <h3>Task Scheduler</h3>
        <p>A DAG-based task graph decomposes complex investigations into subtasks, dispatches them to the right agent type, tracks dependencies, and handles failures &mdash; like a kernel scheduler dispatches threads to CPU cores.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-mem">&#x1F9E0;</div>
        <h3>Memory Management</h3>
        <p>Five layers of cognitive memory (working, episodic, semantic, procedural, RL Q-table) mirror how an OS manages RAM, cache, and swap &mdash; short-term state for active work, long-term storage for learned patterns.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-drv">&#x1F50C;</div>
        <h3>Device Drivers (Environment Adapters)</h3>
        <p>Adapters for Prometheus, Elasticsearch, GitHub, Kubernetes, and Jaeger are the "device drivers" that let HiveANT interface with your infrastructure &mdash; normalizing diverse telemetry into a unified view.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-sec">&#x1F512;</div>
        <h3>Security &amp; Governance</h3>
        <p>JWT/RBAC authentication, policy engine, sandbox execution, approval gates, and immutable audit trails &mdash; the security subsystem ensures agents only do what they're authorized to do.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-ui">&#x1F4CA;</div>
        <h3>Dashboard (User Interface)</h3>
        <p>A real-time web dashboard shows system topology, agent activity, incident timelines, pheromone graphs, and swarm health &mdash; your graphical interface into the operating system.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

      </div>

        <h4 style="color:var(--purple)">Self-Improvement</h4>
        <p>RL parameter tuning</p>
      </div>
      <div class="arch-box" style="background:rgba(139,92,246,.1);border:1px solid rgba(139,92,246,.3)">
        <h4 style="color:var(--purple)">Digital Twin</h4>
        <p>System topology model</p>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="arch-connector"></div>

    <!-- Layer 4: Agents -->
    <div class="arch-label">Layer 4 &mdash; 12 Autonomous Agents</div>
    <div class="arch-layer" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit,minmax(140px,1fr))">
      <div class="arch-box" style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.08);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.3)"><h4 style="color:var(--blue);font-size:12px">Detection</h4></div>
      <div class="arch-box" style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.08);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.3)"><h4 style="color:var(--blue);font-size:12px">Investigation</h4></div>
      <div class="arch-box" style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.08);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.3)"><h4 style="color:var(--blue);font-size:12px">Root Cause</h4></div>
      <div class="arch-box" style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.08);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.3)"><h4 style="color:var(--blue);font-size:12px">Fix Gen</h4></div>

<!-- ══════════════ HOW SWARM WORKS ══════════════ -->
<section style="background:var(--bg2)">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">Swarm Intelligence</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">How ACO + ABC Works</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">Two bio-inspired algorithms work in sequence: ants discover the root cause, bees optimize the fix.</p>
    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:32px;margin-bottom:40px">
      <div style="background:var(--bg);border:1px solid rgba(239,68,68,.3);border-radius:16px;padding:32px">
        <h3 style="color:var(--red);margin-bottom:16px">Phase 1: Ant Colony Optimization</h3>
        <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;margin-bottom:16px">Ants explore causal paths through your system graph. Each ant follows edges weighted by pheromone strength.</p>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num">1</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Explore</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Agents traverse symptom &rarr; cause paths probabilistically</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num">2</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Evaluate</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Each path scored by evidence strength</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num">3</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Reinforce</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Best paths get pheromone boost; weak paths evaporate</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num">4</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Converge</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Swarm converges on highest-probability root cause</p></div></div>
      </div>
      <div style="background:var(--bg);border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,.3);border-radius:16px;padding:32px">
        <h3 style="color:var(--green);margin-bottom:16px">Phase 2: Bee Colony Optimization</h3>
        <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;margin-bottom:16px">Once the root cause is found, bees discover and optimize the best remediation strategy.</p>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num" style="background:var(--green)">1</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Scout</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Scout bees discover diverse fix strategies</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num" style="background:var(--green)">2</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Recruit</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Workers evaluate each strategy for safety &amp; effectiveness</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num" style="background:var(--green)">3</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Evaluate</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Evaluator bees rank by risk, blast radius, and confidence</p></div></div>
        <div class="step"><div class="step-num" style="background:var(--green)">4</div><div class="step-body"><h4>Execute</h4><p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:13px">Best fix is sandbox-tested, then applied with rollback plan</p></div></div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="background:var(--bg);border:1px solid var(--orange);border-radius:16px;padding:24px;text-align:center">
      <h4 style="color:var(--orange);margin-bottom:8px">The Pheromone Graph: Persistent Learning</h4>
      <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;max-width:700px;margin:0 auto">Every resolved incident strengthens causal paths in the pheromone graph. Unused paths naturally evaporate. Over time, the system builds an increasingly accurate map of your infrastructure's failure modes &mdash; making each new investigation faster than the last.</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ══════════════ AGENTS ══════════════ -->
<section id="agents">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">Agents</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">12 Autonomous Agent Types</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">Each agent is specialized for a stage of the incident lifecycle. They communicate via the message bus and coordinate through the task scheduler.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="agents-grid">
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F6E1;</span> Detection Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Monitors system health via Prometheus, Elasticsearch, and HTTP health checks. Fires alerts when anomalies exceed thresholds.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F50D;</span> Investigation Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Collects logs, metrics, traces, and deploy history. Correlates signals across systems to build an investigation timeline.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F41C;</span> Root Cause Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Uses ACO swarm to explore causal paths. Pheromone reinforcement guides the swarm to the most likely root cause.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F41D;</span> Fix Generation Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Uses ABC swarm (Scout/Worker/Evaluator) to discover, evaluate, and rank remediation strategies by safety and effectiveness.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x2705;</span> Validation Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Sandbox-tests proposed fixes in isolation before production. Verifies the fix resolves the issue without side effects.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F4DA;</span> Learning Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Updates all 5 memory layers after resolution: episodic (incident record), semantic (patterns), procedural (runbooks), RL Q-table.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F52E;</span> Prediction Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Forecasts future failures based on current telemetry trends, semantic patterns, and RL Q-values. Proactive, not reactive.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F3D7;</span> Architect Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Analyzes system structure, identifies architectural drift, and recommends improvements for reliability and scalability.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F4BB;</span> Developer Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Generates code patches, configuration changes, and infrastructure-as-code updates based on investigation findings.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F50E;</span> Reviewer Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Automated code review with focus on security vulnerabilities, performance regressions, and correctness verification.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F9EA;</span> Testing Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Generates and executes test suites for proposed changes. Validates fixes don't introduce regressions.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="agent-card">
        <div class="agent-name"><span class="agent-emoji">&#x1F680;</span> Deployment Agent</div>
        <div class="agent-desc">Plans safe rollout strategies (canary, blue-green). Monitors deployment health and auto-rolls back on failure.</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ══════════════ MEMORY ══════════════ -->
<section id="memory" style="background:var(--bg2)">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">Cognitive Memory</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">5-Layer Memory System</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">Inspired by human cognition. Each layer serves a different temporal and functional role, from millisecond working state to permanent learned knowledge.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="memory-stack">
      <div class="memory-layer ml-1">
        <div class="num">1</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Working Memory</h4>
          <p>Current investigation signals, live metrics, in-flight agent state. Cleared after each incident.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="memory-layer ml-2">
        <div class="num">2</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Episodic Memory</h4>
          <p>Complete incident records &mdash; symptoms, timeline, root cause, fix applied, outcome. "What happened."</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="memory-layer ml-3">
        <div class="num">3</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Semantic Memory</h4>
          <p>Generalized patterns extracted from episodes by AI. "Memory leak in service X correlates with deploy of dependency Y."</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="memory-layer ml-4">
        <div class="num">4</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Procedural Memory</h4>
          <p>Learned fix runbooks &mdash; step-by-step procedures that resolved past incidents. Reusable recipes.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="memory-layer ml-5">
        <div class="num">5</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Reinforcement Learning Q-Table</h4>
          <p>Q(state, action) values updated after every resolution. Guides future decisions: which fix to try first, which investigation path to explore.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ══════════════ PREREQUISITES ══════════════ -->
<section id="setup">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header">
      <div class="section-tag">Getting Started</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">What You Need</h2>
    </div>

    <div class="prereqs" style="margin-bottom:48px">
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="required">Required</span></h4>
        <h4>NC Engine</h4>
        <p>The NC runtime that HiveANT is built on. Install from <a href="https://github.com/nicholasgasior/notation-as-code">GitHub</a> or build from source with <code>make</code>. Provides the <code>nc</code> CLI.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="required">Required</span></h4>
        <h4>AI Model</h4>
        <p>Any OpenAI-compatible API. <strong>Recommended:</strong> <a href="https://ollama.com">Ollama</a> running locally with <code>llama3</code>. Free, private, no API keys needed. Also works with OpenAI GPT-4, Claude (via proxy), or any compatible endpoint.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="optional">Optional</span></h4>
        <h4>Prometheus</h4>
        <p>For real-time metrics collection. Detection agents query Prometheus for anomaly detection. Without it, agents use HTTP health checks.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="optional">Optional</span></h4>
        <h4>Elasticsearch</h4>
        <p>For log analysis. Investigation agents search ES for error patterns. Without it, agents analyze local log files.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="optional">Optional</span></h4>
        <h4>GitHub Token</h4>
        <p>For deploy history, PR creation, and code review. Deployment agents use GitHub API for rollback and change management.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="prereq">
        <h4><span class="optional">Optional</span></h4>
        <h4>Docker / Kubernetes</h4>
        <p>For production deployment. Docker Compose for single-node, Kubernetes manifests included for multi-node clusters.</p>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Setup Tabs -->
    <h3 style="margin-bottom:20px">Installation</h3>
    <div class="setup-options">
      <div class="setup-tab active" onclick="showSetup('quick')">Quick Start</div>
      <div class="setup-tab" onclick="showSetup('windows')">Windows</div>
      <div class="setup-tab" onclick="showSetup('docker')">Docker</div>
      <div class="setup-tab" onclick="showSetup('k8s')">Kubernetes</div>
      <div class="setup-tab" onclick="showSetup('manual')">Manual</div>
    </div>

    <div id="setup-quick" class="setup-content active">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">1</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Clone the repository</h4>
          <pre><code>git clone https://github.com/DevHealLabs/hiveant.git
cd hiveant</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">2</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Install Ollama (for local AI)</h4>
          <pre><code># macOS
brew install ollama
ollama serve &amp;
ollama pull llama3

# Linux
curl -fsSL https://ollama.com/install.sh | sh
ollama pull llama3</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">3</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Run setup &amp; start</h4>
          <pre><code>./scripts/setup.sh
./scripts/start.sh

# Or with NC directly:
NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1 NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1 nc run scripts/setup.nc
NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1 NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1 nc serve server.nc</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">4</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Initialize &amp; open dashboard</h4>
          <pre><code>curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/kernel/init
# Open http://localhost:7700 in your browser</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div id="setup-windows" class="setup-content">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">1</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Install Git for Windows (provides required bash shell)</h4>
          <p style="color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:12px">HiveANT uses POSIX shell commands internally. Git for Windows provides the required <code>bash</code>, <code>ls</code>, <code>grep</code>, <code>find</code>, etc.</p>
          <pre><code># Download and install Git for Windows
# https://git-scm.com/download/win
# During install, select "Use Git and optional Unix tools from the Command Prompt"

# Verify bash is in PATH
bash --version</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">2</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Build NC Engine</h4>
          <pre><code># Option A: Using MSYS2/MinGW
pacman -S mingw-w64-x86_64-gcc make
cd nc-main\nc
make

# Option B: Using Visual Studio / CMake
cd nc-main\nc
mkdir build &amp;&amp; cd build
cmake .. &amp;&amp; cmake --build . --config Release</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">3</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Install Ollama for Windows</h4>
          <pre><code># Download from https://ollama.com/download/windows
# After install:
ollama serve
ollama pull llama3</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">4</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Run setup &amp; start (PowerShell)</h4>
          <pre><code># Clone the repo
git clone https://github.com/DevHealLabs/hiveant.git
cd hiveant

# Run setup (checks NC, bash, Ollama, creates directories)
powershell -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File scripts\setup.ps1

# Start HiveANT
powershell -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File scripts\start.ps1

# Or double-click:
scripts\start.bat</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">5</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Initialize &amp; open dashboard</h4>
          <pre><code>curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/kernel/init
# Open http://localhost:7700 in your browser</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div id="setup-docker" class="setup-content">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">1</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Clone and deploy</h4>
          <pre><code>git clone https://github.com/DevHealLabs/hiveant.git
cd hiveant
./scripts/deploy-docker.sh up</code></pre>
          <p>This starts HiveANT + Ollama, pulls the AI model, initializes the kernel, and runs a health check.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">2</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Manage</h4>
          <pre><code>./scripts/deploy-docker.sh logs          # View logs
./scripts/deploy-docker.sh status        # Health check
./scripts/deploy-docker.sh pull-model llama3  # Change model
./scripts/deploy-docker.sh down          # Stop</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div id="setup-k8s" class="setup-content">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">1</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Build &amp; deploy</h4>
          <pre><code>REGISTRY=your-registry.io ./scripts/deploy-k8s.sh build
./scripts/deploy-k8s.sh apply</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">2</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Access &amp; initialize</h4>
          <pre><code>./scripts/deploy-k8s.sh port-forward   # http://localhost:7700
./scripts/deploy-k8s.sh init</code></pre>
          <p>K8s manifests include: Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, Secret, PVC, HPA, Ingress, NetworkPolicy, ServiceAccount + RBAC.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div id="setup-manual" class="setup-content">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">1</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Configure environment</h4>
          <pre><code>cp config/.env.example config/.env
# Edit config/.env with your AI provider, integrations, and security settings</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">2</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Critical environment variables</h4>
          <pre><code># REQUIRED: NC Engine permissions (without these, data is silently lost)
NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1
NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1

# AI Model (pick one)
NC_AI_URL=http://localhost:11434/v1/chat/completions  # Ollama
NC_AI_MODEL=llama3
NC_AI_KEY=local

# Security (generate with: openssl rand -hex 32)
NC_JWT_SECRET=your-secret-here
HIVEANT_PORT=7700</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">3</div>
        <div class="step-body">
          <h4>Start the server</h4>
          <pre><code>NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1 NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1 nc serve server.nc</code></pre>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ══════════════ USE CASES ══════════════ -->
<section id="use-cases">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">Use Cases</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">Real-World Applications</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">HiveANT is designed for any team that operates software systems at scale.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="use-cases">
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>Cloud Infrastructure (SRE/DevOps)</h3>
        <div class="problem">100+ microservices, 3 AM alert storms, hours of manual debugging</div>
        <div class="solution">Detection agents spot anomalies. ACO finds root cause in minutes. ABC generates the optimal fix. Learning agents ensure the same issue resolves faster next time. Example: a deploy changes DB credentials &rarr; HiveANT detects 94% error spike, traces the causal chain, recommends rollback in 60 seconds.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>Financial Trading Platforms</h3>
        <div class="problem">Zero latency tolerance &mdash; 50ms increase can cost millions</div>
        <div class="solution">Sub-millisecond anomaly detection. Causal reasoning identifies whether issue is network, app, or data-feed. Prediction agents forecast degradation before it impacts trades. Self-healing with zero-downtime rollback.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>Healthcare System Reliability</h3>
        <div class="problem">99.99% uptime required, cascading failures endanger patient safety</div>
        <div class="solution">Digital twin models all service dependencies. Impact analysis shows blast radius. Sandbox validation ensures fixes don't create new problems. Audit trail provides regulatory compliance documentation.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>E-Commerce (Peak Traffic)</h3>
        <div class="problem">Black Friday cascading failures, manual scaling too slow</div>
        <div class="solution">Prediction agents forecast traffic and pre-scale. Detection catches emerging issues before customers notice. ABC finds fastest remediation (scale pods, enable CDN, rate limit) and applies automatically.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>CI/CD Pipeline Intelligence</h3>
        <div class="problem">Flaky tests, build failures, deployment rollbacks waste time</div>
        <div class="solution">Testing agents analyze failure patterns. Deployment agents plan safe rollouts. Prediction flags risky PRs before merge. Learning builds "what breaks and why" knowledge base.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="use-case">
        <h3>Cybersecurity Incident Response</h3>
        <div class="problem">Breaches need rapid cross-system investigation</div>
        <div class="solution">Detection identifies anomalous patterns. Investigation correlates security events. Causal reasoning builds attack chain graphs. Sandbox validates containment before execution.</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ══════════════ SECURITY HARDENING ══════════════ -->
<section id="security" style="background:var(--bg)">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">Security</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">Production-Grade Hardening</h2>
      <p class="section-desc">24 tracked issues identified, 22 resolved. Every security-sensitive code path has been audited and patched.</p>
    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit,minmax(280px,1fr));gap:20px;margin-bottom:40px">
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-sec">&#x1F6E1;</div>
        <h3>Shell Injection Prevention</h3>
        <p>All user inputs pass through <code>sanitize()</code> before shell interpolation. Dangerous characters (<code>; | $ ` &amp;</code>) are stripped. AI-generated commands are validated against an allowlist of safe executables.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-kernel">&#x1F512;</div>
        <h3>Path Traversal Protection</h3>
        <p><code>validate_path()</code> and <code>safe_id()</code> reject <code>..</code>, <code>/</code>, and <code>\</code> in all user-supplied IDs. Plugin names, entity IDs, and agent IDs are all sanitized before file path construction.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-sched">&#x1F504;</div>
        <h3>Race Condition Prevention</h3>
        <p>File-based locking (<code>acquire_lock</code> / <code>release_lock</code>) protects all read-modify-write sections. Kernel state, pheromone graph, and scheduler are safe under concurrent load.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-mem">&#x1F9E0;</div>
        <h3>NC Engine Fixes</h3>
        <p>GC marking optimized from O(N&sup2;) to O(1) via pointer hash table. Thread-safe GC threshold checks. Buffer pooling eliminates server heap churn. YAML parser fully rewritten. Windows path normalization added.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-drv">&#x1F50D;</div>
        <h3>Input Validation</h3>
        <p>CORS configurable via <code>HIVEANT_CORS_ORIGIN</code>. SSRF protection blocks metadata endpoints. JWT authentication with HS256. RBAC roles (admin, operator, viewer). Immutable audit trail for every action.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="os-card">
        <div class="icon icon-ui">&#x2705;</div>
        <h3>Module Robustness</h3>
        <p><code>file_exists</code> guards before every <code>read_file</code>. <code>try/otherwise</code> error handling for JSON parsing. Proper array responses from all list endpoints. Plugin and knowledge graph sanitization.</p>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="max-width:700px;margin:0 auto">
      <h3 style="margin-bottom:16px;text-align:center">Issue Resolution Status</h3>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:24px;justify-content:center;margin-bottom:24px">
        <div style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:36px;font-weight:800;color:var(--green)">22</span><br><span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2)">Fixed</span></div>
        <div style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:36px;font-weight:800;color:var(--amber)">2</span><br><span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2)">Open</span></div>
        <div style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:36px;font-weight:800;color:var(--blue)">24</span><br><span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2)">Total</span></div>
      </div>
      <p style="text-align:center;color:var(--text2);font-size:14px">Remaining: <code>json_decode</code> error handling (mitigated with try/otherwise) and expanded test coverage. See <a href="https://github.com/DevHealLabs/hiveant/blob/main/docs/NC_ISSUES.md">NC_ISSUES.md</a> for full details.</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

        </p>
      </div>
      <div style="border-left:3px solid var(--green);padding-left:24px;margin-bottom:32px">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom:8px">Security Hardening (22 Fixes)</h3>
        <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;line-height:1.8">
          &bull; Shell injection prevention: <code>sanitize()</code>, <code>safe_id()</code>, <code>validate_path()</code>, <code>validate_command()</code><br>
          &bull; Race condition prevention via file-based locking<br>
          &bull; Path traversal protection on all user-supplied IDs<br>
          &bull; AI command allowlist (only <code>kubectl</code>, <code>docker</code>, <code>systemctl</code>, etc.)<br>

        <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;line-height:1.8">
          &bull; GC marking: O(N&sup2;) &rarr; O(1) via pointer hash table<br>
          &bull; Thread-safe GC threshold check<br>
          &bull; HTTP response buffer pooling (eliminates malloc/free per request)<br>
          &bull; Dynamic query string allocation (no more 512-byte truncation)<br>
          &bull; Redaction cache (one-time env var resolution)<br>
          &bull; Full YAML parser rewrite (nested objects, lists, type detection)
        </p>

      <div style="border-left:3px solid var(--purple);padding-left:24px;margin-bottom:32px">

        <p style="color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;line-height:1.8">
          &bull; Pheromone evaporation now properly decays and prunes edges<br>
          &bull; Pheromone query returns actual results (was always empty)<br>
          &bull; Plugin list returns proper JSON arrays (was malformed)<br>
          &bull; Bus topics returns array with count (was raw string)<br>
          &bull; All modules have <code>file_exists</code> guards and <code>try/otherwise</code> blocks<br>
          &bull; Knowledge graph and incident DB sanitize all inputs<br>
          &bull; Plugin register signature aligned across server and SDK
        </p>

          &bull; Issue-specific tests for all 22 original bugs
        </p>

<!-- ══════════════ FAQ ══════════════ -->
<section id="faq" style="background:var(--bg2)">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header center">
      <div class="section-tag">FAQ</div>
      <h2 class="section-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
    </div>
    <div style="max-width:800px;margin:0 auto">
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What AI model does HiveANT need?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Any OpenAI-compatible API. We recommend Ollama with llama3 for local, free, private inference. You can also use OpenAI GPT-4, Anthropic Claude (via a compatible proxy), or any provider that exposes <code>/v1/chat/completions</code>. Configure via <code>NC_AI_URL</code>, <code>NC_AI_MODEL</code>, and <code>NC_AI_KEY</code> in your .env file.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Is HiveANT safe to use in production?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">HiveANT includes multiple safety layers: sandbox testing before production execution, command allowlists for AI-generated actions, approval gates for high-risk operations, blast radius analysis via digital twin, and rollback plans. The <code>REQUIRE_APPROVAL_FOR=high-risk</code> setting ensures dangerous actions always require human approval. Start in read-only mode (viewer role) to observe before granting execution permissions.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Can it run without Prometheus/Elasticsearch?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Yes. All environment integrations are optional. Without Prometheus, detection agents fall back to HTTP health checks and AI-based analysis. Without Elasticsearch, investigation agents analyze local logs. The core swarm intelligence, memory system, and agent coordination work independently of external tools.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">How does pheromone evaporation work?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Every causal edge in the pheromone graph has a score. When an investigation confirms a causal path, the score is reinforced (multiplied by a boost factor). On a decay cycle, every edge score is multiplied by <code>(1 - PHEROMONE_DECAY_RATE)</code>. Edges below <code>PHEROMONE_MIN_THRESHOLD</code> are pruned. This ensures the graph stays current &mdash; frequently confirmed patterns remain strong while stale relationships naturally fade.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What is NC Engine?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">NC (Notation as Code) is a plain-English programming language with AI as a native instruction. HiveANT is written entirely in NC. The NC runtime compiles plain English into bytecode and executes it on a lightweight C VM (~570KB binary). NC has a built-in HTTP server, file I/O, JSON handling, and an <code>ask AI</code> opcode that calls any AI provider natively. This is why HiveANT code reads like English specifications rather than traditional code.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Can I scale to 10,000+ agents?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Yes. HiveANT uses hierarchical swarm clustering: agents are organized into clusters (default 100 clusters, 100 agents each = 10,000). Each cluster operates independently for local issues, while a global coordinator shares patterns across clusters. Configure with <code>HIVEANT_MAX_AGENTS</code>, <code>HIVEANT_CLUSTERS</code>, and <code>HIVEANT_AGENTS_PER_CLUSTER</code>.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What license is HiveANT under?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">MIT License. Use it freely for personal, commercial, or enterprise purposes. Contributions welcome &mdash; see CONTRIBUTING.md.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Does HiveANT work on Windows?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Yes. As of v1.1.0, HiveANT has full Windows support. The NC engine compiles natively on Windows (MSYS2/MinGW or Visual Studio/CMake) with WinHTTP for HTTP calls (no libcurl dependency). HiveANT's server uses POSIX shell commands internally, so you need Git for Windows (recommended) or MSYS2 installed to provide <code>bash</code>, <code>ls</code>, <code>grep</code>, etc. Run <code>scripts\setup.ps1</code> to verify your environment, or double-click <code>scripts\start.bat</code> to launch.</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">How is this different from LangChain/CrewAI/AutoGen?<span class="arrow">&#x25BC;</span></div>
        <div class="faq-a"><div class="faq-a-inner">Those are general-purpose agent frameworks. HiveANT is a purpose-built <strong>operating system for infrastructure operations</strong>. Key differences: (1) Bio-inspired swarm algorithms (ACO/ABC) vs. sequential chains, (2) Persistent pheromone graph that improves with every incident, (3) 5-layer cognitive memory vs. simple context windows, (4) Built-in environment adapters for Prometheus/ES/K8s/GitHub, (5) Security-first with sandbox, approval gates, and audit trails, (6) Digital twin with blast radius analysis. LangChain helps you build chatbots; HiveANT runs your infrastructure.</div></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<script>
function showSetup(id){
  document.querySelectorAll('.setup-content').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.setup-tab').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('setup-'+id).classList.add('active');
  event.target.classList.add('active');
}

function toggleFaq(el){
  el.parentElement.classList.toggle('open');
}

// Smooth scroll for nav links
document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(a=>{
  a.addEventListener('click',e=>{
    e.preventDefault();
    const t=document.querySelector(a.getAttribute('href'));
    if(t)t.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});
    document.getElementById('nav').classList.remove('open');
  });
});

// Nav background on scroll
window.addEventListener('scroll',()=>{
  document.querySelector('nav').style.borderBottomColor=window.scrollY>50?'rgba(30,30,58,.8)':'rgba(30,30,58,.3)';
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
const A='';
const $=id=>document.getElementById(id);
const J=(o)=>JSON.stringify(o,null,2);
let JWT_TOKEN=localStorage.getItem('hiveant_jwt')||'';
let CURRENT_USER=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('hiveant_user')||'null');

async function api(m,p,b){
  const o={method:m,headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}};
  if(JWT_TOKEN){
    if(m==='POST'){
      if(!b)b={};
      b.token=JWT_TOKEN;
    }else if(m==='GET'&&p.startsWith('/auth/')){
      o.method='POST';
      b={token:JWT_TOKEN};
    }
  }
  if(b)o.body=JSON.stringify(b);
  try{
    const r=await fetch(A+p,o);
    const d=await r.json();
    if(d._status===401&&!p.includes('/auth/login')){showLogin();return d;}
    if(d._status===403){toast('Access denied: '+(d.error||'insufficient permissions'),'error');return d;}
    return d;
  }catch(e){return{error:e.message};}
}

function nav(page){
  document.querySelectorAll('[id^="page-"]').forEach(p=>p.classList.add('hidden'));
  $('page-'+page).classList.remove('hidden');
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n=>n.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelector(`.nav-item[data-page="${page}"]`).classList.add('active');
}
document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n=>n.addEventListener('click',()=>nav(n.dataset.page)));

function toast(msg,type='info'){
  const t=document.createElement('div');
  t.className='toast toast-'+type;
  t.textContent=msg;
  $('toasts').appendChild(t);
  setTimeout(()=>t.remove(),4000);
}

function swarmTab(t,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  el.classList.add('active');
  $('stab-ant').classList.toggle('hidden',t!=='ant');
  $('stab-bee').classList.toggle('hidden',t!=='bee');
}

function renderInvestigation(r){
  if(r.error){$('inv-results').innerHTML=`<div class="panel"><div class="result-card"><h4>Error</h4><p>${r.error}</p></div></div>`;return;}
  let h='';
  h+=`<div class="panel"><div class="panel-title">Root Cause Analysis</div>`;
  h+=`<div class="result-card"><h4>Root Cause</h4><p style="font-size:15px;color:var(--text);font-weight:600">${r.root_cause||'Unknown'}</p>`;
  h+=`<div style="display:flex;gap:16px;margin-top:10px"><div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">CONFIDENCE</span><div class="metric" style="color:${(r.confidence||0)>70?'var(--green)':'var(--accent)'}">${r.confidence||0}%</div></div>`;
  h+=`<div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">CATEGORY</span><div style="margin-top:4px"><span class="tag tag-medium">${r.category||'unknown'}</span></div></div>`;
  h+=`<div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">INCIDENT</span><div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:13px;margin-top:4px;color:var(--accent)">${r.incident_id||'—'}</div></div></div></div>`;
  if(r.causal_chain&&r.causal_chain.length>0){
    h+=`<div class="result-card"><h4>Causal Chain</h4><div class="causal-chain">`;
    r.causal_chain.forEach((n,i)=>{
      if(i>0)h+=`<span class="causal-arrow">→</span>`;
      h+=`<span class="causal-node ${n.type||''}">${n.node||n}</span>`;
    });
    h+=`</div></div>`;
  }
  h+=`</div>`;
  if(r.remediation&&r.remediation.recommended_fix){
    const fix=r.remediation.recommended_fix;
    h+=`<div class="panel"><div class="panel-title">Recommended Fix</div>`;
    h+=`<div class="result-card"><h4>${fix.solution_id||'Fix'} — ${fix.category||''}</h4><p>${fix.description||''}</p>`;
    if(fix.commands&&fix.commands.length>0){
      h+=`<div style="margin-top:12px">`;
      fix.commands.forEach(c=>{
        h+=`<div class="fix-step"><span class="step-num">${c.step||'•'}</span><div><code>${c.cmd||''}</code><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:2px">${c.description||''} <span class="tag tag-${c.risk||'low'}">${c.risk||'low'}</span></p></div></div>`;
      });
      h+=`</div>`;
    }
    h+=`<div style="margin-top:10px"><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">CONFIDENCE</span> <strong>${fix.confidence_percent||0}%</strong> &nbsp; <span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">RISK</span> <span class="tag tag-${fix.risk_level||'low'}">${fix.risk_level||'low'}</span></div>`;
    h+=`</div></div>`;
  }
  $('inv-results').innerHTML=h;
  $('inv-raw-panel').style.display='block';
  $('inv-raw').textContent=J(r);
}

async function initKernel(){
  $('dash-output').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/kernel/init');
  $('dash-output').textContent=J(r);
  toast('Kernel initialized','success');
  refreshDashboard();
}

async function refreshDashboard(){
  try{
    const[status,ph,k]=await Promise.all([api('GET','/kernel/status'),api('GET','/pheromone/status'),api('GET','/knowledge')]);
    if(status.kernel&&!status.error){
      $('s-agents').textContent=status.kernel.agent_count||'0';
      $('s-incidents').textContent=status.incidents||'0';
      if(!CURRENT_USER) updateUserBadge();
      $('sys-badge').className='badge badge-healthy';
      $('sys-badge').innerHTML='<span class="dot"></span> Healthy';
    }else if(status.error){
      $('sys-badge').className='badge badge-error';
      $('sys-badge').innerHTML='<span class="dot"></span> Not Initialized';
    }
    $('s-pheromone').textContent=ph.edges||'0';
    if(k.semantic&&k.semantic!=='none'){try{$('s-patterns').textContent=JSON.parse(k.semantic).total||'0';}catch(e){$('s-patterns').textContent='0';}}
    else{$('s-patterns').textContent='0';}
    $('dash-output').textContent=J(status);
  }catch(e){
    $('sys-badge').className='badge badge-error';
    $('sys-badge').innerHTML='<span class="dot"></span> Disconnected';
  }
}

async function deepHealth(){
  $('dash-output').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('GET','/health/deep');
  $('dash-output').textContent=J(r);
  toast(r.status||'Health check complete','info');
}

async function runWatchdog(){
  $('dash-output').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/watchdog');
  $('dash-output').textContent=J(r);
  toast('Watchdog scan complete','info');
}

async function loadSample(){
  const r=await api('GET','/sample');
  $('inv-svc').value=r.service_name||'';
  $('inv-desc').value=r.description||'';
  toast('Sample data loaded','success');
}

async function investigate(){
  const svc=$('inv-svc').value,desc=$('inv-desc').value;
  if(!svc||!desc)return toast('Enter service name and description','error');
  $('inv-results').innerHTML='<div class="panel"><div class="loading-bar"></div><p style="text-align:center;color:var(--text2);padding:20px">Swarm investigating... ACO exploring causal paths, ABC optimizing fixes. This takes 30-120 seconds.</p></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/investigate',{service_name:svc,description:desc});
  if(r._status===503||r.error&&r.error.includes('AI')){
    $('inv-results').innerHTML=`<div class="panel"><div class="result-card" style="border-color:var(--red)"><h4 style="color:var(--red)">AI Model Unavailable</h4><p>${r.error||'AI model is not reachable. Start Ollama or configure NC_AI_URL.'}</p><p style="margin-top:10px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text3)">Fix: <code>ollama serve</code> then <code>ollama pull llama3</code></p></div></div>`;
    toast('AI model not available','error');
  }else{
    renderInvestigation(r);
    toast('Investigation complete','success');
  }
}

async function selfHeal(){
  const svc=$('inv-svc').value,desc=$('inv-desc').value;
  if(!svc||!desc)return toast('Enter service name and description','error');
  $('inv-results').innerHTML='<div class="panel"><div class="loading-bar"></div><p style="text-align:center;color:var(--text2);padding:20px">Self-healing in progress...</p></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/self-heal',{service_name:svc,description:desc,auto_execute:'no'});
  $('inv-results').innerHTML='';
  $('inv-raw-panel').style.display='block';
  $('inv-raw').textContent=J(r);
  toast('Self-heal analysis complete','success');
}

async function loadIncidents(){
  const r=await api('GET','/incidents');
  if(!r.incidents||r.incidents.length===0){
    $('incidents-list').innerHTML='<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">▣</div><p>No incidents yet.</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  let h='<div class="panel-title">Recent Incidents <span class="count">'+r.count+'</span></div>';
  r.incidents.forEach(id=>{
    h+=`<div class="incident-row" onclick="loadIncident('${id}')"><div><span class="inc-id">${id}</span></div><div class="btn btn-outline btn-sm">View</div></div>`;
    h+=`<div class="incident-detail" id="detail-${id}"></div>`;
  });
  $('incidents-list').innerHTML=h;
}

async function loadIncident(id){
  const el=$('detail-'+id);
  if(el.classList.contains('open')){el.classList.remove('open');return;}
  document.querySelectorAll('.incident-detail').forEach(d=>d.classList.remove('open'));
  el.innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  el.classList.add('open');
  const r=await api('POST','/incident',{incident_id:id});
  if(r.error){el.innerHTML=`<p style="color:var(--red)">${r.error}</p>`;return;}
  let h=`<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:12px">`;
  h+=`<div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">ROOT CAUSE</span><p style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600">${r.root_cause||'—'}</p></div>`;
  h+=`<div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">CONFIDENCE</span><p style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;color:var(--accent)">${r.confidence||0}%</p></div>`;
  h+=`<div><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">CATEGORY</span><p><span class="tag tag-medium">${r.category||'—'}</span></p></div></div>`;
  h+=`<div style="margin-top:12px"><span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">SERVICE</span> <strong>${r.service||'—'}</strong> &nbsp; <span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">DURATION</span> <strong>${(r.duration_seconds||0).toFixed(1)}s</strong></div>`;
  h+=`<div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;gap:8px"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="sendFeedback('${id}','yes')">✓ Correct</button><button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="sendFeedback('${id}','no')">✗ Incorrect</button></div>`;
  h+=`<details style="margin-top:12px"><summary style="cursor:pointer;color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">Full JSON</summary><div class="output" style="margin-top:8px;max-height:300px">${J(r)}</div></details>`;
  el.innerHTML=h;
}

async function sendFeedback(id,correct){
  const r=await api('POST','/feedback',{incident_id:id,correct:correct,notes:correct==='yes'?'Confirmed via dashboard':'Marked incorrect via dashboard'});
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');return;}
  toast(correct==='yes'?'Feedback: Root cause confirmed. Knowledge updated.':'Feedback: Marked incorrect. Will improve.', correct==='yes'?'success':'info');
}

async function spawnAgent(){
  const r=await api('POST','/agents/spawn',{agent_type:$('agent-type').value,agent_id:$('agent-id').value||undefined});
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');return;}
  toast('Agent spawned: '+r.id,'success');
  loadAgents();
}

async function loadAgents(){
  const r=await api('GET','/agents');
  const agents=Array.isArray(r.agents)?r.agents:[];
  if(agents.length===0){$('agents-grid').innerHTML='<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">⬡</div><p>No agents running.</p></div>';$('agent-count').textContent='0';return;}
  $('agent-count').textContent=agents.length;
  $('agents-grid').innerHTML=agents.map(a=>`<div class="agent-chip"><div class="type">${a.type||'unknown'}</div><div class="aid">${a.id||'?'}</div><div class="chip-footer"><span class="tag tag-${a.status||'unknown'}">${a.status||'unknown'}</span>${a.status==='running'?`<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="killAgent('${a.id}')">Kill</button>`:''}</div></div>`).join('');
}

async function killAgent(id){
  await api('POST','/agents/kill',{agent_id:id});
  toast('Agent terminated: '+id,'info');
  loadAgents();
}

async function antExplore(){
  $('ant-out').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/swarm/ant/explore',{signals:$('ant-sig').value,system_context:$('ant-ctx').value});
  $('ant-out').textContent=J(r);
  toast('ACO exploration complete','success');
}

async function beeOptimize(){
  $('bee-out').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/swarm/bee/optimize',{root_cause:$('bee-cause').value,system_context:$('bee-ctx').value});
  $('bee-out').textContent=J(r);
  toast('ABC optimization complete','success');
}

async function loadPheromone(){const r=await api('GET','/pheromone/status');$('ph-stats').textContent=J(r);}
async function addEdge(){
  const r=await api('POST','/pheromone/add',{from_node:$('ph-from').value,to_node:$('ph-to').value,score:parseFloat($('ph-score').value)||1.0});
  toast('Edge added: '+($('ph-from').value)+'→'+($('ph-to').value),'success');
  loadPheromone();
}
async function loadKnowledge(){const r=await api('GET','/knowledge');$('know-out').textContent=J(r);}
async function predict(){
  $('pred-out').innerHTML='<div class="loading-bar"></div>';
  const r=await api('POST','/predict',{service_name:$('pred-svc').value,time_horizon:$('pred-hr').value||'24h'});
  $('pred-out').textContent=J(r);
}
async function twinReg(){
  const r=await api('POST','/twin/register',{service_name:$('tw-name').value,service_type:$('tw-type').value});
  toast('Service registered','success');
  loadTwin();
}
async function loadTwin(){const r=await api('GET','/twin/topology');$('twin-out').textContent=J(r);}
async function loadAudit(){const r=await api('GET','/audit');$('audit-out').textContent=J(r);}

async function sendChat(){
  const msg=$('chat-in').value;if(!msg)return;
  $('chat-in').value='';
  $('chat-msgs').innerHTML+=`<div class="chat-bubble user"><div class="sender">You</div>${msg}</div>`;
  $('chat-msgs').innerHTML+=`<div class="chat-bubble assistant" id="chat-pending"><div class="sender">HiveANT</div><span class="spinner"></span> Thinking...</div>`;
  $('chat-msgs').scrollTop=$('chat-msgs').scrollHeight;
  const r=await api('POST','/chat',{message:msg});
  const reply=typeof r.reply==='string'?r.reply:J(r.reply||r);
  $('chat-pending').innerHTML=`<div class="sender">HiveANT</div>${reply}`;
  $('chat-pending').removeAttribute('id');
  $('chat-msgs').scrollTop=$('chat-msgs').scrollHeight;
}

function showLogin(){
  if($('login-overlay'))return;
  const ov=document.createElement('div');
  ov.id='login-overlay';
  ov.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.9);z-index:2000;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center';
  ov.innerHTML=`<div style="background:var(--surface);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:16px;padding:32px;width:400px;box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,.6)">
    <h2 style="font-size:20px;margin-bottom:4px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">🐜 HiveANT</h2>
    <p style="color:var(--text3);font-size:12px;margin-bottom:20px">Sign in to access the Swarm AI OS</p>
    <div class="tabs" id="login-tabs" style="margin-bottom:16px">
      <div class="tab active" onclick="loginTab('user',this)">Username</div>
      <div class="tab" onclick="loginTab('apikey',this)">API Key</div>
    </div>
    <div id="login-user-form">
      <div class="form-group"><label>Username</label><input class="input" id="login-username" placeholder="admin" autocomplete="username"></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>Password</label><input class="input" id="login-password" type="password" placeholder="Password" autocomplete="current-password" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')doLogin()"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="login-apikey-form" style="display:none">
      <div class="form-group"><label>API Key</label><input class="input" id="login-key" type="password" placeholder="HIVEANT_API_KEY" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')doLogin()"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="login-error" style="color:var(--red);font-size:12px;margin-bottom:10px;display:none"></div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:8px">
      <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="doLogin()" style="flex:1">Sign In</button>
      <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="skipLogin()">Read-Only</button>
    </div>
    <p style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px;margin-top:14px;text-align:center">First time? Register via CLI: <code style="color:var(--cyan);font-size:10px">POST /auth/register</code></p>
  </div>`;
  document.body.appendChild(ov);
  setTimeout(()=>$('login-username')&&$('login-username').focus(),100);
}

let loginMode='user';
function loginTab(mode,el){
  loginMode=mode;
  document.querySelectorAll('#login-tabs .tab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('active'));
  el.classList.add('active');
  $('login-user-form').style.display=mode==='user'?'block':'none';
  $('login-apikey-form').style.display=mode==='apikey'?'block':'none';
}

async function doLogin(){
  let body={};
  if(loginMode==='user'){
    const u=$('login-username').value,p=$('login-password').value;
    if(!u||!p){$('login-error').textContent='Username and password required';$('login-error').style.display='block';return;}
    body={username:u,password:p};
  }else{
    const k=$('login-key').value;
    if(!k){$('login-error').textContent='API key required';$('login-error').style.display='block';return;}
    body={api_key:k};
  }
  const r=await fetch(A+'/auth/login',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify(body)}).then(r=>r.json()).catch(()=>({error:'Connection failed'}));
  if(r.authenticated&&r.token){
    JWT_TOKEN=r.token;
    CURRENT_USER={user:r.user,role:r.role};
    localStorage.setItem('hiveant_jwt',r.token);
    localStorage.setItem('hiveant_user',JSON.stringify(CURRENT_USER));
    $('login-overlay').remove();
    updateUserBadge();
    toast('Signed in as '+r.user+' ('+r.role+')','success');
  }else{
    $('login-error').textContent=r.error||'Authentication failed';
    $('login-error').style.display='block';
  }
}

function skipLogin(){
  $('login-overlay').remove();
  CURRENT_USER={user:'anonymous',role:'viewer'};
  updateUserBadge();
  toast('Read-only mode — sign in for write access','info');
}

function logout(){
  JWT_TOKEN='';
  CURRENT_USER=null;
  localStorage.removeItem('hiveant_jwt');
  localStorage.removeItem('hiveant_user');
  updateUserBadge();
  toast('Signed out','info');
}

function updateUserBadge(){
  if(CURRENT_USER){
    $('conn-status').className='conn-status ok';
    $('conn-status').innerHTML=`<span class="dot"></span> ${CURRENT_USER.user} <span class="tag tag-${CURRENT_USER.role==='admin'?'low':CURRENT_USER.role==='operator'?'medium':'high'}" style="margin-left:4px">${CURRENT_USER.role}</span> <span style="cursor:pointer;margin-left:auto;font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)" onclick="logout()">Sign Out</span>`;
  }else{
    $('conn-status').className='conn-status';
    $('conn-status').innerHTML='<span class="dot"></span> Not signed in';
  }
}

async function checkAuth(){
  const r=await fetch(A+'/auth/status').then(r=>r.json()).catch(()=>({auth_required:false}));
  if(r.auth_required&&!JWT_TOKEN){
    showLogin();
  }else if(JWT_TOKEN&&CURRENT_USER){
    updateUserBadge();
  }else if(!r.auth_required){
    CURRENT_USER={user:'anonymous',role:'admin'};
    updateUserBadge();
  }
}

async function loadAuthStatus(){
  const r=await api('GET','/auth/status');
  $('settings-auth-status').textContent=J(r);
}
async function registerUser(){
  const u=$('reg-user').value,p=$('reg-pass').value,rl=$('reg-role').value,org=$('reg-org').value;
  if(!u||!p)return toast('Username and password required','error');
  const r=await api('POST','/auth/register',{username:u,password:p,role:rl,org_id:org,admin_token:JWT_TOKEN});
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');}else{toast('User '+u+' registered ('+rl+')','success');loadUsers();}
}
async function loadUsers(){
  const r=await api('GET','/auth/users');
  if(r.error){$('users-list').innerHTML=`<p style="color:var(--red)">${r.error}</p>`;return;}
  if(!r.users||r.users.length===0){$('users-list').innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--text3)">No users</p>';return;}
  $('user-total').textContent=r.count;
  let h='';
  r.users.forEach(u=>{
    h+=`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">
      <div><strong>${u.username}</strong> <span class="tag tag-${u.role==='admin'?'low':u.role==='operator'?'medium':'high'}">${u.role}</span> <span class="tag tag-${u.status==='active'?'low':'critical'}">${u.status}</span> <span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px;margin-left:8px">${u.org_id||'default'}</span></div>
      <div class="btn-group">
        ${u.status==='active'?`<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="updateUser('${u.username}','','disabled')">Disable</button>`:`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="updateUser('${u.username}','','active')">Enable</button>`}
        <button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="if(confirm('Delete ${u.username}?'))deleteUser('${u.username}')">Delete</button>
      </div></div>`;
  });
  $('users-list').innerHTML=h;
}
async function updateUser(u,role,status){
  const b={target_username:u,token:JWT_TOKEN};
  if(role)b.new_role=role;
  if(status)b.new_status=status;
  const r=await api('POST','/auth/users/update',b);
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');}else{toast('User '+u+' updated','success');loadUsers();}
}
async function deleteUser(u){
  const r=await api('POST','/auth/users/delete',{target_username:u,token:JWT_TOKEN});
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');}else{toast('User '+u+' deleted','info');loadUsers();}
}
async function changePassword(){
  const cur=$('cp-current').value,nw=$('cp-new').value;
  if(!cur||!nw)return toast('Both fields required','error');
  const r=await api('POST','/auth/change-password',{current_password:cur,new_password:nw,token:JWT_TOKEN});
  if(r.error){toast(r.error,'error');}else{toast('Password changed','success');$('cp-current').value='';$('cp-new').value='';}
}
async function loadOrgs(){
  const r=await api('GET','/auth/orgs');
  $('orgs-list').textContent=J(r);
}

async function refreshToken(){
  if(!JWT_TOKEN||JWT_TOKEN==='no-auth-configured')return;
  const r=await fetch(A+'/auth/refresh',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({token:JWT_TOKEN})}).then(r=>r.json()).catch(()=>null);
  if(r&&r.token){
    JWT_TOKEN=r.token;
    localStorage.setItem('hiveant_jwt',r.token);
  }
}

checkAuth();
refreshDashboard();
setInterval(()=>{if(!document.querySelector('#page-dashboard.hidden'))refreshDashboard();},30000);
setInterval(refreshToken,300000);
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!-- Overview -->
<section id="overview">
  <div class="container">
    <h2 class="section-title">What is <span class="accent">HiveANT</span>?</h2>
    <p class="section-sub">A self-healing infrastructure system that thinks like a colony.</p>
    <p class="overview-text">
      HiveANT is a <strong>multi-agent autonomous incident response system</strong> inspired by
      <strong>ant colony intelligence</strong>. It deploys specialized AI agents that collaboratively
      detect anomalies, investigate root causes, generate fixes, validate changes, and learn from
      every incident &mdash; all without human intervention. Built entirely in
      <strong>NC</strong>, HiveANT brings swarm intelligence to site reliability engineering,
      turning your infrastructure into a self-healing organism.
    </p>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- Features -->
<section id="features">
  <div class="container">
    <h2 class="section-title">Key <span class="accent">Features</span></h2>
    <p class="section-sub">Everything you need for autonomous incident response, out of the box.</p>
    <div class="features-grid">

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#129514;</div>
        <h3>12 Specialized Agent Types</h3>
        <p>Detection, Investigation, Root Cause Analysis, Fix Generation, Validation, Learning, Prediction, Architect, Developer, Reviewer, Testing, and Deployment agents working in concert.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#128028;</div>
        <h3>Ant Colony Optimization</h3>
        <p>ACO-based distributed decision-making lets agents lay pheromone trails to converge on optimal incident resolution paths, just like real ant colonies.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#127855;</div>
        <h3>Artificial Bee Colony</h3>
        <p>ABC algorithm optimizes resource allocation across agents, balancing exploration of new solutions with exploitation of known-good remediation strategies.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#129504;</div>
        <h3>5-Layer Cognitive Memory</h3>
        <p>Working memory, episodic memory, semantic knowledge, procedural skills, and reinforcement learning layers give agents deep contextual understanding.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#127760;</div>
        <h3>Digital Twin Analysis</h3>
        <p>Simulate changes against a digital twin of your infrastructure to predict blast radius before any fix is applied to production.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#128274;</div>
        <h3>JWT/RBAC Security</h3>
        <p>Fine-grained role-based access control with JWT authentication and comprehensive audit logging for every agent action and remediation step.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#128200;</div>
        <h3>Real-Time Dashboard</h3>
        <p>Live visualization of agent swarm activity, incident timelines, resolution metrics, and system health across your entire infrastructure.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="icon">&#9889;</div>
        <h3>Written Entirely in NC</h3>
        <p>The entire HiveANT system is built in NC, a language designed for high-performance systems programming with built-in safety and concurrency.</p>
      </div>

    </div>
  </div>
</section>

  <span class="hl-cyan">Prometheus</span>    <span class="hl-cyan">Elasticsearch</span>    <span class="hl-cyan">Jaeger</span>    <span class="hl-cyan">Kubernetes</span>

                         |                |
            +------------+---+---+--------+----------+
            |                |                       |
     <span class="hl-orange">+------+------+  +------+------+  +----------+--------+</span>

                     |                   |

                     |                   |
                     +---------+---------+
                               |
                    <span class="hl-orange">+----------+----------+</span>

                    <span class="hl-orange">+----------+----------+</span>
                               |
                    <span class="hl-cyan">+----------+----------+</span>
                    <span class="hl-cyan">|   Learning Agent    |</span>
                    <span class="hl-cyan">|  (5-Layer Memory)   |</span>
                    <span class="hl-cyan">+---------------------+</span>

  <span class="hl-white">ACO Engine</span> ............. Distributed decision-making across all agents
  <span class="hl-white">ABC Engine</span> ............. Resource optimization &amp; workload balancing
  <span class="hl-white">Digital Twin</span> ........... Blast-radius simulation before deployment
  <span class="hl-white">Audit Logger</span> ........... JWT/RBAC secured action logging</div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- How it works -->
<section id="how-it-works">
  <div class="container">
    <h2 class="section-title">How It <span class="accent">Works</span></h2>
    <p class="section-sub">Six stages from anomaly to resolution, fully autonomous.</p>
    <div class="steps">
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">1</div>
        <h4>Detect</h4>
        <p>Agents monitor metrics, logs, and traces in real time to identify anomalies.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">2</div>
        <h4>Investigate</h4>
        <p>Investigation agents gather context, correlate signals, and build an incident profile.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">3</div>
        <h4>Diagnose</h4>
        <p>Root cause analysis pinpoints the underlying failure using cognitive memory layers.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">4</div>
        <h4>Fix</h4>
        <p>Architect, developer, and reviewer agents collaborate to generate a verified remediation.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">5</div>
        <h4>Validate</h4>
        <p>Testing and validation agents verify the fix against the digital twin before deployment.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="num">6</div>
        <h4>Learn</h4>
        <p>The learning agent stores patterns across all five memory layers for future incidents.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

      HiveANT is written from the ground up in <strong style="color:var(--white)">NC</strong> &mdash;
      a systems programming language engineered for performance, safety, and native concurrency.
      NC's lightweight runtime and deterministic memory model make it ideal for orchestrating
      swarms of AI agents with minimal overhead and maximum reliability.

<!-- Quick Start -->
<section id="quickstart">
  <div class="container">
    <h2 class="section-title">Quick <span class="accent">Start</span></h2>
    <p class="section-sub">Get HiveANT running in minutes.</p>
    <div class="code-block"><span class="comment"># Clone the repository</span>
<span class="cmd">git clone</span> <span class="arg">https://github.com/user/hiveant.git</span>
<span class="cmd">cd</span> hiveant

<span class="comment"># Build with NC</span>
<span class="cmd">nc build</span> <span class="arg">--release</span>

<span class="comment"># Configure your integrations</span>
<span class="cmd">cp</span> config.example.nc <span class="arg">config.nc</span>
<span class="comment"># Edit config.nc with your Prometheus, K8s, and GitHub endpoints</span>

<span class="comment"># Start the HiveANT swarm</span>
<span class="cmd">nc run</span> <span class="arg">hiveant --mode autonomous</span>

<span class="comment"># Open the dashboard</span>
<span class="comment"># http://localhost:8420</span></div>
  </div>
</section>

<canvas id="bg"></canvas>
<div class="pulse"></div>
<div class="content">
  <div class="code">404</div>
  <div class="title">Neural pathway not found</div>
  <div class="subtitle">The requested route does not exist in this model's weights.</div>
  <a href="/" class="home-btn">Return to NC AI</a>

<script>
const c=document.getElementById('bg'),x=c.getContext('2d');
function resize(){c.width=innerWidth;c.height=innerHeight}
resize();addEventListener('resize',resize);
const dots=[];
for(let i=0;i<50;i++)dots.push({x:Math.random()*c.width,y:Math.random()*c.height,vx:(Math.random()-.5)*.5,vy:(Math.random()-.5)*.5,r:2});
function draw(){
  x.clearRect(0,0,c.width,c.height);
  dots.forEach(d=>{
    d.x+=d.vx;d.y+=d.vy;
    if(d.x<0||d.x>c.width)d.vx*=-1;
    if(d.y<0||d.y>c.height)d.vy*=-1;
    x.beginPath();x.arc(d.x,d.y,d.r,0,Math.PI*2);
    x.fillStyle='rgba(0,212,255,.6)';x.fill();
  });
  for(let i=0;i<dots.length;i++)for(let j=i+1;j<dots.length;j++){
    const dx=dots[i].x-dots[j].x,dy=dots[i].y-dots[j].y,dist=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
    if(dist<150){x.beginPath();x.moveTo(dots[i].x,dots[i].y);x.lineTo(dots[j].x,dots[j].y);
    x.strokeStyle=`rgba(124,58,237,${1-dist/150})`;x.lineWidth=.5;x.stroke();}
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(draw);
}
draw();
</script>

        </div>

        <p>Send NC code prompts to any external teacher LLM. The teacher generates high-quality code. NC AI's student model trains on it and absorbs the teacher's patterns.</p>
      </div>

        <div class="feature-icon" style="background:rgba(192,38,211,.08)">

        </div>
