<!-- ======== SCRIPTS ======== -->
<script>
/* ---- Neural Network Canvas ---- */
(function(){
  const canvas=document.getElementById('heroCanvas');
  const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');
  let w,h,nodes=[],mouse={x:null,y:null};
  const NODE_COUNT=window.innerWidth<768?40:80;
  const CONNECT_DIST=window.innerWidth<768?120:160;

  function resize(){
    w=canvas.width=canvas.offsetWidth;
    h=canvas.height=canvas.offsetHeight;
  }
  resize();
  window.addEventListener('resize',resize);

  for(let i=0;i<NODE_COUNT;i++){
    nodes.push({
      x:Math.random()*w,
      y:Math.random()*h,
      vx:(Math.random()-.5)*.6,
      vy:(Math.random()-.5)*.6,
      r:Math.random()*2+1,
      pulse:Math.random()*Math.PI*2
    });
  }

  canvas.addEventListener('mousemove',e=>{
    const r=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    mouse.x=e.clientX-r.left;
    mouse.y=e.clientY-r.top;
  });
  canvas.addEventListener('mouseleave',()=>{mouse.x=null;mouse.y=null});

  function draw(){
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h);
    const t=Date.now()*.001;

    nodes.forEach(n=>{
      n.x+=n.vx;n.y+=n.vy;
      if(n.x<0||n.x>w)n.vx*=-1;
      if(n.y<0||n.y>h)n.vy*=-1;

      if(mouse.x!==null){
        const dx=n.x-mouse.x,dy=n.y-mouse.y,d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
        if(d<200){n.x+=dx/d*.5;n.y+=dy/d*.5;}
      }

      const p=Math.sin(t+n.pulse)*.5+.5;
      const alpha=.3+p*.4;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(n.x,n.y,n.r+p,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(0,212,255,${alpha})`;
      ctx.fill();
    });

    for(let i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){
      for(let j=i+1;j<nodes.length;j++){
        const dx=nodes[i].x-nodes[j].x;
        const dy=nodes[i].y-nodes[j].y;
        const d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
        if(d<CONNECT_DIST){
          const alpha=(1-d/CONNECT_DIST)*.2;
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(nodes[i].x,nodes[i].y);
          ctx.lineTo(nodes[j].x,nodes[j].y);
          ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(124,58,237,${alpha})`;
          ctx.lineWidth=.6;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  }
  draw();
})();

/* ---- Scroll reveal ---- */
const reveals=document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
const io=new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
  entries.forEach(e=>{if(e.isIntersecting){e.target.classList.add('visible');io.unobserve(e.target);}});
},{threshold:.15});
reveals.forEach(el=>io.observe(el));

/* ---- Nav scroll ---- */
window.addEventListener('scroll',()=>{
  document.getElementById('nav').classList.toggle('scrolled',window.scrollY>50);
});

/* ---- Hamburger ---- */
document.getElementById('hamburger').addEventListener('click',function(){
  document.getElementById('navLinks').classList.toggle('open');
  this.classList.toggle('active');
});
document.querySelectorAll('#navLinks a').forEach(a=>{
  a.addEventListener('click',()=>{document.getElementById('navLinks').classList.remove('open');});
});

/* ---- Terminal animation ---- */
(function(){
  const body=document.getElementById('terminalBody');
  const cursor=document.getElementById('termCursor');
  let started=false;

  const lines=[
    {text:'$ nc ai generate "a blog service with auth and dark dashboard"',cls:'cmd',delay:40},
    {text:'',cls:'',delay:600},
    {text:'[nc_metal] GPU initialized: Apple M1 Pro',cls:'info',delay:0,pause:400},
    {text:'\u2819 Loading model (dim=256, 6 layers, 4096 vocab)...',cls:'info',delay:0,pause:800},
    {text:'\u2819 Encoding prompt (BPE tokenizer)...',cls:'info',delay:0,pause:400},
    {text:'\u2819 Generating tokens (temperature=0.7)...',cls:'info',delay:0,pause:1200},
    {text:'',cls:'',delay:300},
    {text:'service "blog-api"',cls:'file',delay:0,pause:200},
    {text:'version "1.0.0"',cls:'file',delay:0,pause:150},
    {text:'',cls:'',delay:100},
    {text:'to create_post with data:',cls:'file',delay:0,pause:200},
    {text:'    store data into "posts"',cls:'file',delay:0,pause:150},
    {text:'    respond with {"status": "created"}',cls:'file',delay:0,pause:150},
    {text:'',cls:'',delay:200},
    {text:'\u2713 Generated 42 tokens in 0.3s (Metal GPU)',cls:'success',delay:0},
  ];

  function typeWriter(text,el,cls,charDelay){
    return new Promise(resolve=>{
      if(charDelay===0||charDelay===undefined&&text.length===0){
        const span=document.createElement('span');
        if(cls)span.className=cls;
        span.textContent=text;
        body.insertBefore(span,cursor);
        body.insertBefore(document.createElement('br'),cursor);
        resolve();
        return;
      }
      let i=0;
      const span=document.createElement('span');
      if(cls)span.className=cls;
      body.insertBefore(span,cursor);
      function type(){
        if(i<text.length){
          span.textContent+=text[i];i++;
          setTimeout(type,charDelay);
        }else{
          body.insertBefore(document.createElement('br'),cursor);
          resolve();
        }
      }
      type();
    });
  }

  function sleep(ms){return new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms));}

  async function runDemo(){
    body.innerHTML='';
    body.appendChild(cursor);
    for(const line of lines){
      await typeWriter(line.text,body,line.cls,line.delay);
      if(line.pause)await sleep(line.pause);
      else await sleep(150);
    }
    cursor.style.display='none';
    await sleep(4000);
    cursor.style.display='';
    runDemo();
  }

  const observer=new IntersectionObserver(entries=>{
    if(entries[0].isIntersecting&&!started){
      started=true;
      runDemo();
    }
  },{threshold:.3});
  observer.observe(body);
})();

/* ---- Copy install ---- */
function copyInstall(){
  const text='curl -sSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nc-lang/nc/main/install.sh | bash\nnc ai generate "a todo app with dark theme"\nnc ai status';
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(()=>{
    const btn=document.getElementById('copyBtn');
    btn.textContent='Copied!';
    btn.classList.add('copied');
    setTimeout(()=>{btn.textContent='Copy';btn.classList.remove('copied');},2000);
  });
}
</script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
(function(){
  // Scroll-driven animations via IntersectionObserver
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(entry){
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        // Stagger children
        const parent = entry.target.closest('[class*=ncui-anim-stagger]');
        if(parent){
          const siblings = Array.from(entry.target.parentElement.children);
          const idx = siblings.indexOf(entry.target);
          entry.target.style.transitionDelay = (idx * 0.1) + 's';
        }
        entry.target.classList.add('ncui-visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.1,rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});

  // Observe all section direct children and grid children
  document.querySelectorAll('[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-container > *, [class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-grid > .ncui-card').forEach(function(el){
    obs.observe(el);
  });

  // Smooth nav background
  var nav = document.querySelector('.ncui-nav');
  if(nav){
    window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      if(window.scrollY > 50) nav.style.padding = '10px 0';
      else nav.style.padding = '16px 0';
    },{passive:true});
  }

  // Form submission handler
  document.querySelectorAll('.ncui-form').forEach(function(form){
    form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var btn = form.querySelector('.ncui-btn');
      if(btn){
        var orig = btn.textContent;
        btn.textContent = 'Sent!';
        btn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
        setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent = orig; btn.style.pointerEvents='auto';},2000);
      }
    });
  });
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<section class="problem" id="problem">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-center">
      <span class="section-label reveal">The Problem</span>
      <h2 class="section-title reveal reveal-delay-1">Building AI APIs<br>shouldn't require <span class="grad">7 packages</span></h2>
      <p class="section-desc reveal reveal-delay-2">Python needs Flask, OpenAI, dotenv, gunicorn, CORS, rate-limiters, and more. NC needs one file.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="problem-grid">
      <div class="problem-panel old glass-card reveal">
        <h3>The Python Way</h3>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install flask</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install openai</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install python-dotenv</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install flask-cors</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install flask-limiter</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install gunicorn</div>
        <div class="stack-item">pip install pyjwt</div>
      </div>
      <div class="problem-arrow reveal">&rarr;</div>
      <div class="problem-panel new glass-card reveal">
        <h3>The NC Way</h3>
        <div class="stack-item">nc run api.nc</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="counters">
      <div class="counter-item glass-card reveal">
        <div class="counter-val"><span class="count-up" data-target="7">0</span> &rarr; <span class="count-up" data-target="1">0</span></div>
        <div class="counter-label">Packages needed</div>
        <div class="counter-detail">7 pip installs vs 1 file</div>
      </div>
      <div class="counter-item glass-card reveal reveal-delay-1">
        <div class="counter-val"><span class="count-up" data-target="120">0</span> &rarr; <span class="count-up" data-target="12">0</span></div>
        <div class="counter-label">Lines of code</div>
        <div class="counter-detail">For an AI-powered API</div>
      </div>
      <div class="counter-item glass-card reveal reveal-delay-2">
        <div class="counter-val"><span class="count-up" data-target="35">0</span>MB &rarr; <span class="count-up" data-target="570">0</span>KB</div>
        <div class="counter-label">Runtime size</div>
        <div class="counter-detail">60x smaller footprint</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ════════════ LIVE CODE COMPARISON ════════════ -->
<section class="code-compare" id="compare">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-center">
      <span class="section-label reveal">Code Comparison</span>
      <h2 class="section-title reveal reveal-delay-1">See the <span class="grad">difference</span></h2>
      <p class="section-desc reveal reveal-delay-2">The same AI classification API. Left is Python + Flask. Right is NC.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="compare-grid reveal">
      <div class="compare-panel dimmed">
        <div class="panel-header">
          <span class="panel-title">classify_api.py</span>
          <span class="panel-badge python">Python + Flask</span>
        </div>
<pre><span class="cm"># classify_api.py</span>
<span class="kw">import</span> os
<span class="kw">from</span> flask <span class="kw">import</span> Flask, request, jsonify
<span class="kw">from</span> flask_cors <span class="kw">import</span> CORS
<span class="kw">from</span> flask_limiter <span class="kw">import</span> Limiter
<span class="kw">from</span> flask_limiter.util <span class="kw">import</span> get_remote_address
<span class="kw">import</span> openai
<span class="kw">from</span> dotenv <span class="kw">import</span> load_dotenv

load_dotenv()
app = Flask(__name__)
CORS(app)

limiter = Limiter(
    app=app,
    key_func=get_remote_address,
    default_limits=[<span class="str">"100 per minute"</span>]
)

openai.api_key = os.getenv(<span class="str">"OPENAI_API_KEY"</span>)

<span class="deco">@app.route</span>(<span class="str">"/classify"</span>, methods=[<span class="str">"POST"</span>])
<span class="kw">def</span> <span class="fn">classify</span>():
    data = request.get_json()
    text = data.get(<span class="str">"text"</span>, <span class="str">""</span>)

    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
        model=<span class="str">"gpt-4"</span>,
        messages=[{
            <span class="str">"role"</span>: <span class="str">"user"</span>,
            <span class="str">"content"</span>: <span class="kw">f</span><span class="str">"Classify: {text}"</span>
        }]
    )

    result = response.choices[<span class="num">0</span>].message.content
    <span class="kw">return</span> jsonify({<span class="str">"result"</span>: result})

<span class="kw">if</span> __name__ == <span class="str">"__main__"</span>:
    app.run(
        host=<span class="str">"0.0.0.0"</span>,
        port=<span class="num">3000</span>,
        debug=<span class="kw">False</span>
    )</pre>
        <div class="line-count">45 lines &middot; 7 dependencies</div>
      </div>

      <div class="compare-panel highlighted">
        <div class="panel-header">
          <span class="panel-title">classify.nc</span>
          <span class="panel-badge nc">NC</span>
        </div>
<pre><span class="cm">// classify.nc</span>

<span class="kw">create</span> <span class="fn">server</span>
<span class="kw">enable</span> <span class="fn">cors</span>
<span class="kw">enable</span> <span class="fn">rate_limit</span> <span class="num">100</span> <span class="kw">per</span> <span class="str">"minute"</span>

<span class="kw">listen</span> <span class="fn">POST</span> <span class="str">"/classify"</span>
    <span class="kw">set</span> text <span class="kw">to</span> body.text

    <span class="ai">ask AI to</span> <span class="str">"Classify this text as
    positive, negative, or neutral: {text}"</span>

    <span class="kw">send</span> AI.response
<span class="kw">end</span>

<span class="kw">start</span> <span class="fn">server</span> <span class="kw">on port</span> <span class="num">3000</span></pre>
        <div class="line-count">12 lines &middot; 0 dependencies</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- ════════════ FEATURES ════════════ -->
<section id="features">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-center">
      <span class="section-label reveal">Features</span>
      <h2 class="section-title reveal reveal-delay-1">Everything you need,<br><span class="grad">nothing you don't</span></h2>
      <p class="section-desc reveal reveal-delay-2">NC ships as a single binary with batteries included. No frameworks, no package managers, no configuration files.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="features-grid">
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#9997;&#65039;</div>
        <h3>Plain English Syntax</h3>
        <p>Write code that reads like natural language. No semicolons, no braces, no cryptic symbols. If you can describe it, you can code it.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-1">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#129302;</div>
        <h3>AI as a Native Instruction</h3>
        <p>Use <code style="color:var(--cyan)">ask AI to</code> anywhere in your code. AI isn't a library &mdash; it's a first-class language feature.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-2">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#9889;</div>
        <h3>Built-in HTTP Server</h3>
        <p>Create production-ready APIs with zero setup. No Express, no Flask, no external servers needed.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-3">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#128230;</div>
        <h3>80+ Built-in Functions</h3>
        <p>String manipulation, file I/O, JSON parsing, encryption, hashing &mdash; all included out of the box.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-4">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#129504;</div>
        <h3>Built-in LLM</h3>
        <p>World's first language with its own transformer model. <code style="color:var(--cyan)">nc ai generate</code> converts English to complete applications.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-5">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#9889;</div>
        <h3>Metal GPU Accelerated</h3>
        <p>AI engine uses Metal Performance Shaders + Apple Accelerate BLAS. 50-100x faster than naive CPU on Apple Silicon.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#129519;</div>
        <h3>~600KB Binary</h3>
        <p>The entire NC runtime with built-in AI is under 600KB. No runtime, no VM, no interpreter chain. Just download and run.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card glass-card reveal reveal-delay-1">
        <div class="feature-icon">&#127760;</div>
        <h3>Cross-Platform</h3>
        <p>Runs natively on macOS, Linux, and Windows. Same code, same behavior, every platform.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

          <span>form.nc</span>
          <span class="ui-coming-soon">Coming Soon</span>
        </div>
<pre><span class="cm">// form.nc — build UI in plain English</span>

<span class="kw">create</span> <span class="fn">page</span> <span class="str">"Contact Us"</span>

<span class="kw">add</span> <span class="fn">heading</span> <span class="str">"Get in Touch"</span>

    <span class="kw">placeholder</span> <span class="str">"Enter your name"</span>
<span class="kw">end</span>

<span class="kw">add</span> <span class="fn">input</span> <span class="str">"Email"</span>
    <span class="kw">placeholder</span> <span class="str">"you@example.com"</span>

    <span class="kw">style</span> <span class="str">"primary"</span>
    <span class="kw">on click</span> <span class="fn">submit_form</span>

      </div>

<script>
/* ── PARTICLE CANVAS ── */
(function() {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('particle-canvas');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  let particles = [];
  let w, h, animFrame;
  let isVisible = true;

  function resize() {
    w = canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    h = canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
  }

  function createParticles() {
    particles = [];
    const count = Math.min(Math.floor((w * h) / 18000), 80);
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      particles.push({
        x: Math.random() * w,
        y: Math.random() * h,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3,
        vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3,
        r: Math.random() * 1.5 + 0.5,
        o: Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.1
      });
    }
  }

  function draw() {
    if (!isVisible) { animFrame = requestAnimationFrame(draw); return; }
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

    for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
      const p = particles[i];
      p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;
      if (p.x < 0) p.x = w; if (p.x > w) p.x = 0;
      if (p.y < 0) p.y = h; if (p.y > h) p.y = 0;

      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 212, 255, ' + p.o + ')';
      ctx.fill();

      /* Connect nearby particles */
      for (let j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
        const p2 = particles[j];
        const dx = p.x - p2.x, dy = p.y - p2.y;
        const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
        if (dist < 15000) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(p.x, p.y);
          ctx.lineTo(p2.x, p2.y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 212, 255, ' + (0.06 * (1 - dist / 15000)) + ')';
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
    }
    animFrame = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  }

  /* Pause when hero not visible */
  const heroObs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    isVisible = entries[0].isIntersecting;
  }, { threshold: 0 });
  heroObs.observe(document.querySelector('.hero'));

  window.addEventListener('resize', function() { resize(); createParticles(); });
  resize();
  createParticles();
  draw();
})();

/* ── TYPING ANIMATION ── */
(function() {
  const lines = [
    { text: '// classify.nc', cls: 'cm' },
    { text: '', cls: '' },
    { text: 'create ', cls: 'kw', extra: [{ text: 'server', cls: 'fn' }] },
    { text: '', cls: '' },
    { text: 'listen ', cls: 'kw', extra: [{ text: 'POST', cls: 'fn' }, { text: ' ', cls: '' }, { text: '"/classify"', cls: 'str' }] },
    { text: '    set ', cls: 'kw', extra: [{ text: 'text ', cls: '' }, { text: 'to', cls: 'kw' }, { text: ' body.text', cls: '' }] },
    { text: '', cls: '' },
    { text: '    ask AI to', cls: 'ai', extra: [{ text: ' ', cls: '' }, { text: '"Classify: {text}"', cls: 'str' }] },
    { text: '    send ', cls: 'kw', extra: [{ text: 'AI.response', cls: '' }] },
    { text: 'end', cls: 'kw' },
    { text: '', cls: '' },
    { text: 'start ', cls: 'kw', extra: [{ text: 'server', cls: 'fn' }, { text: ' ', cls: '' }, { text: 'on port', cls: 'kw' }, { text: ' ', cls: '' }, { text: '3000', cls: 'num' }] }
  ];

  const container = document.getElementById('typed-code');
  let lineIdx = 0, charIdx = 0, currentSpans = [];
  let currentLine, cursor;

  function buildSpans(line) {
    const spans = [];
    if (line.cls) {
      spans.push({ text: line.text, cls: line.cls });
    } else {
      spans.push({ text: line.text, cls: '' });
    }
    if (line.extra) {
      for (const e of line.extra) spans.push(e);
    }
    return spans;
  }

  function flatText(spans) {
    return spans.map(function(s) { return s.text; }).join('');
  }

  function renderUpTo(lineIndex, charIndex) {
    let html = '';
    /* Already completed lines */
    for (let i = 0; i < lineIndex; i++) {
      const spans = buildSpans(lines[i]);
      for (const s of spans) {
        if (s.cls) html += '<span class="' + s.cls + '">' + escHtml(s.text) + '</span>';
        else html += escHtml(s.text);
      }
      html += '\n';
    }
    /* Current line up to charIndex */
    if (lineIndex < lines.length) {
      const spans = buildSpans(lines[lineIndex]);
      const full = flatText(spans);
      let written = 0;
      for (const s of spans) {
        const start = written;
        const end = written + s.text.length;
        if (charIndex <= start) break;
        const slice = s.text.substring(0, charIndex - start);
        if (s.cls) html += '<span class="' + s.cls + '">' + escHtml(slice) + '</span>';
        else html += escHtml(slice);
        written = end;
        if (charIndex <= end) break;
      }
    }
    html += '<span class="cursor"></span>';
    container.innerHTML = html;
  }

  function escHtml(t) {
    return t.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
  }

  function typeNext() {
    if (lineIdx >= lines.length) {
      /* Done; restart after pause */
      setTimeout(function() { lineIdx = 0; charIdx = 0; container.innerHTML = '<span class="cursor"></span>'; setTimeout(typeNext, 500); }, 4000);
      return;
    }
    const spans = buildSpans(lines[lineIdx]);
    const full = flatText(spans);
    if (charIdx <= full.length) {
      renderUpTo(lineIdx, charIdx);
      charIdx++;
      setTimeout(typeNext, full.length === 0 ? 150 : 35 + Math.random() * 25);
    } else {
      lineIdx++; charIdx = 0;
      setTimeout(typeNext, 80);
    }
  }

  setTimeout(typeNext, 1500);
})();

/* ── SCROLL REVEAL (IntersectionObserver) ── */
(function() {
  const els = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(e) {
      if (e.isIntersecting) {
        e.target.classList.add('visible');
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.1, rootMargin: '0px 0px -40px 0px' });
  els.forEach(function(el) { obs.observe(el); });
})();

/* ── COUNTER ANIMATION ── */
(function() {
  const counters = document.querySelectorAll('.count-up');
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(e) {
      if (e.isIntersecting && !e.target.dataset.done) {
        e.target.dataset.done = '1';
        const target = parseInt(e.target.dataset.target);
        const duration = 1500;
        const start = performance.now();
        function tick(now) {
          const elapsed = now - start;
          const progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
          /* Ease out cubic */
          const eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
          e.target.textContent = Math.floor(eased * target);
          if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
          else e.target.textContent = target;
        }
        requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.3 });
  counters.forEach(function(c) { obs.observe(c); });
})();

/* ── BAR ANIMATION ── */
(function() {
  const bars = document.querySelectorAll('.bar-fill');
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(e) {
      if (e.isIntersecting) {
        e.target.classList.add('animate');
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.2 });
  bars.forEach(function(b) { obs.observe(b); });
})();

/* ── MAGNETIC BUTTONS ── */
(function() {
  var btns = document.querySelectorAll('.magnetic');
  btns.forEach(function(btn) {
    btn.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
      var rect = btn.getBoundingClientRect();
      var x = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2;
      var y = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2;
      btn.style.transform = 'translate(' + (x * 0.15) + 'px, ' + (y * 0.15) + 'px)';
    });
    btn.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
      btn.style.transform = '';
    });
  });
})();

/* ── INSTALL TABS ── */
function showInstall(idx) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.install-tab').forEach(function(t, i) {
    t.classList.toggle('active', i === idx);
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('.install-cmd-box').forEach(function(b, i) {
    b.classList.toggle('active', i === idx);
  });
}

/* ── COPY COMMAND ── */
function copyCmd(btn, text) {
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(function() {
    btn.textContent = 'Copied!';
    btn.classList.add('copied');
    setTimeout(function() { btn.textContent = 'Copy'; btn.classList.remove('copied'); }, 2000);
  });
}

/* ── PARALLAX (subtle, on hero glow) ── */
(function() {
  var glow = document.querySelector('.hero-glow');
  var ticking = false;
  window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    if (!ticking) {
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        var scroll = window.pageYOffset;
        if (scroll < window.innerHeight) {
          glow.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, calc(-50% + ' + (scroll * 0.15) + 'px))';
        }
        ticking = false;
      });
      ticking = true;
    }
  });
})();

/* ── CLOSE MOBILE NAV ON LINK CLICK ── */
document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links a').forEach(function(a) {
  a.addEventListener('click', function() {
    document.querySelector('.nav-links').classList.remove('open');
  });
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
(function(){
  // Scroll-driven animations
  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(entry){
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        var parent=entry.target.closest('[class*=ncui-anim-stagger]');
        if(parent){
          var siblings=Array.from(entry.target.parentElement.children);
          var idx=siblings.indexOf(entry.target);
          entry.target.style.transitionDelay=(idx*0.1)+'s';
        }
        entry.target.classList.add('ncui-visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.1,rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});

  document.querySelectorAll('[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-container>*,[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-grid>.ncui-card').forEach(function(el){
    obs.observe(el);
  });

  // Nav scroll effect
  var nav=document.querySelector('.ncui-nav');
  if(nav){
    window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      nav.style.padding=window.scrollY>50?'10px 0':'16px 0';
    },{passive:true});
  }

  // Form handler
  document.querySelectorAll('.ncui-form').forEach(function(form){
    if(form.hasAttribute('data-ncui-submit'))return;
    form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var btn=form.querySelector('.ncui-btn');
      if(btn){var orig=btn.textContent;btn.textContent='Sent!';btn.style.pointerEvents='none';setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent=orig;btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'},2000);}
    });
  });

  // Tab switching
  window.ncuiSwitchTab=function(groupId,idx){
    var panels=document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab-group="'+groupId+'"]');
    var tabsEl=document.getElementById(groupId);
    if(!tabsEl)return;
    var btns=tabsEl.querySelectorAll('.ncui-tab-btn');
    for(var i=0;i<panels.length;i++){
      panels[i].style.display=i===idx?'':'none';
    }
    for(var j=0;j<btns.length;j++){
      btns[j].classList.toggle('ncui-tab-active',j===idx);
    }
  };
})();
</script>
<script></script>

<script>
(function(){
  // Scroll-driven animations
  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(entry){
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        var parent=entry.target.closest('[class*=ncui-anim-stagger]');
        if(parent){
          var siblings=Array.from(entry.target.parentElement.children);
          var idx=siblings.indexOf(entry.target);
          entry.target.style.transitionDelay=(idx*0.1)+'s';
        }
        entry.target.classList.add('ncui-visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.1,rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});

  document.querySelectorAll('[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-container>*,[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-grid>.ncui-card').forEach(function(el){
    obs.observe(el);
  });

  // Nav scroll effect
  var nav=document.querySelector('.ncui-nav');
  if(nav){
    window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      nav.style.padding=window.scrollY>50?'10px 0':'16px 0';
    },{passive:true});
  }

  // Form handler
  document.querySelectorAll('.ncui-form').forEach(function(form){
    if(form.hasAttribute('data-ncui-submit'))return;
    form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var btn=form.querySelector('.ncui-btn');
      if(btn){var orig=btn.textContent;btn.textContent='Sent!';btn.style.pointerEvents='none';setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent=orig;btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'},2000);}
    });
  });

  // Tab switching
  window.ncuiSwitchTab=function(groupId,idx){
    var panels=document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab-group="'+groupId+'"]');
    var tabsEl=document.getElementById(groupId);
    if(!tabsEl)return;
    var btns=tabsEl.querySelectorAll('.ncui-tab-btn');
    for(var i=0;i<panels.length;i++){
      panels[i].style.display=i===idx?'':'none';
    }
    for(var j=0;j<btns.length;j++){
      btns[j].classList.toggle('ncui-tab-active',j===idx);
    }
  };
})();
</script>
<script></script>

<script>
(function(){
  // Scroll-driven animations
  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(entry){
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        var parent=entry.target.closest('[class*=ncui-anim-stagger]');
        if(parent){
          var siblings=Array.from(entry.target.parentElement.children);
          var idx=siblings.indexOf(entry.target);
          entry.target.style.transitionDelay=(idx*0.1)+'s';
        }
        entry.target.classList.add('ncui-visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.1,rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});

  document.querySelectorAll('[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-container>*,[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-grid>.ncui-card').forEach(function(el){
    obs.observe(el);
  });

  // Nav scroll effect
  var nav=document.querySelector('.ncui-nav');
  if(nav){
    window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      nav.style.padding=window.scrollY>50?'10px 0':'16px 0';
    },{passive:true});
  }

  // Form handler
  document.querySelectorAll('.ncui-form').forEach(function(form){
    if(form.hasAttribute('data-ncui-submit'))return;
    form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var btn=form.querySelector('.ncui-btn');
      if(btn){var orig=btn.textContent;btn.textContent='Sent!';btn.style.pointerEvents='none';setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent=orig;btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'},2000);}
    });
  });

  // Tab switching
  window.ncuiSwitchTab=function(groupId,idx){
    var panels=document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab-group="'+groupId+'"]');
    var tabsEl=document.getElementById(groupId);
    if(!tabsEl)return;
    var btns=tabsEl.querySelectorAll('.ncui-tab-btn');
    for(var i=0;i<panels.length;i++){
      panels[i].style.display=i===idx?'':'none';
    }
    for(var j=0;j<btns.length;j++){
      btns[j].classList.toggle('ncui-tab-active',j===idx);
    }
  };
})();
</script>
<script></script>

<script>
(function(){
  // Scroll-driven animations
  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(entry){
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        var parent=entry.target.closest('[class*=ncui-anim-stagger]');
        if(parent){
          var siblings=Array.from(entry.target.parentElement.children);
          var idx=siblings.indexOf(entry.target);
          entry.target.style.transitionDelay=(idx*0.1)+'s';
        }
        entry.target.classList.add('ncui-visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.1,rootMargin:'0px 0px -40px 0px'});

  document.querySelectorAll('[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-container>*,[class*=ncui-anim-] .ncui-grid>.ncui-card').forEach(function(el){
    obs.observe(el);
  });

  // Nav scroll effect
  var nav=document.querySelector('.ncui-nav');
  if(nav){
    window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      nav.style.padding=window.scrollY>50?'10px 0':'16px 0';
    },{passive:true});
  }

  // Form handler
  document.querySelectorAll('.ncui-form').forEach(function(form){
    if(form.hasAttribute('data-ncui-submit'))return;
    form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var btn=form.querySelector('.ncui-btn');
      if(btn){var orig=btn.textContent;btn.textContent='Sent!';btn.style.pointerEvents='none';setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent=orig;btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'},2000);}
    });
  });

  // Tab switching
  window.ncuiSwitchTab=function(groupId,idx){
    var panels=document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab-group="'+groupId+'"]');
    var tabsEl=document.getElementById(groupId);
    if(!tabsEl)return;
    var btns=tabsEl.querySelectorAll('.ncui-tab-btn');
    for(var i=0;i<panels.length;i++){
      panels[i].style.display=i===idx?'':'none';
    }
    for(var j=0;j<btns.length;j++){
      btns[j].classList.toggle('ncui-tab-active',j===idx);
    }
  };
})();
</script>
<script>(function(){
var _state={};
_state["tasks"]=null;
_state["filter"]="all";
_state["darkMode"]=true;
var _listeners=[];
function _get(k){return _state[k]}
function _set(k,v){_state[k]=v;_notify()}
function _toggle(k){_state[k]=!_state[k];_notify()}
function _addTo(k,v){if(Array.isArray(_state[k]))_state[k].push(v);_notify()}
function _notify(){
  _listeners.forEach(function(fn){fn(_state)});
  // Update data-ncui-text
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-ncui-text]').forEach(function(el){
    var tpl=el.getAttribute('data-ncui-text');
    el.textContent=tpl.replace(/\{\{([^}]+)\}\}/g,function(_,e){
      var v=_state[e.trim()];return v!=null?v:'';
    });
  });
  // Update data-ncui-if
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-ncui-if]').forEach(function(el){
    var k=el.getAttribute('data-ncui-if');
    var neg=k.charAt(0)==='!';
    var rk=neg?k.slice(1):k;
    var show=neg?!_state[rk]:!!_state[rk];
    el.style.display=show?'':'none';
  });
}
function action_addTask(text){
  _addTo("tasks",text);
}
function action_removeTask(index){
}
function action_setFilter(value){
  _set("filter",value);
}
document.querySelectorAll('[data-ncui-click]').forEach(function(el){
  el.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    var name=el.getAttribute('data-ncui-click');
    var fn=window['action_'+name]||eval('typeof action_'+name+'==="function"&&action_'+name);
    if(typeof fn==='function')fn();
  });
});
document.querySelectorAll('[data-ncui-submit]').forEach(function(form){
  form.addEventListener('submit',function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    var name=form.getAttribute('data-ncui-submit');
    var fn=window['action_'+name]||eval('typeof action_'+name+'==="function"&&action_'+name);
    if(typeof fn==='function')fn();
  });
});
window.action_addTask=action_addTask;
window.action_removeTask=action_removeTask;
window.action_setFilter=action_setFilter;
})();
</script>
</body>

    // ─── Examples ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    const EXAMPLES = {
      portfolio: `page "John Doe — Portfolio"
theme "dark"
accent "#00d4ff"

nav:
    brand "JD"
    links:
        link "Work" to "#work"
        link "About" to "#about"
        link "Contact" to "#contact"

section hero centered:
    badge "Available for hire"
    heading "John Doe" style "gradient"
    subheading "Full Stack Developer & Designer"
    text "I craft modern web experiences with clean code and beautiful interfaces. Let's build something extraordinary together."

        button "View My Work" links to "#work" style "primary"

            heading "Deployments"
            stat "342" "This month"
            text "Up 23% from last month"
        card icon "shield":
            heading "Uptime"
            stat "99.98%" "Last 90 days"
            text "Zero critical incidents"
        card icon "heart":
            heading "NPS Score"
            stat "72" "Industry avg: 44"
            text "Customer satisfaction rising"
    animate "stagger"

    text "Analytics Dashboard v2.4 — Built with NC UI"
    row:
        link "Documentation" to "#"
        link "Support" to "#"
        link "Status" to "#"`

    // ─── DOM ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    const editor = document.getElementById('editor');
    const preview = document.getElementById('preview');
    const errorBar = document.getElementById('errorBar');
    const lineCount = document.getElementById('lineCount');
    const compileTime = document.getElementById('compileTime');
    const exampleSelect = document.getElementById('exampleSelect');
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');

    // ─── Compile ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    let compileTimer = null;
    let lastCompiledHtml = '';

    function compileAndRender() {
      const source = editor.value;
      const lines = source.split('\n').length;
      lineCount.textContent = lines + ' line' + (lines === 1 ? '' : 's');

      try {
        const start = performance.now();
        const html = NCUI.compile(source);
        const elapsed = (performance.now() - start).toFixed(1);
        compileTime.textContent = elapsed + 'ms';

        lastCompiledHtml = html;

        const doc = preview.contentDocument || preview.contentWindow.document;
        doc.open();
        doc.write(html);
        doc.close();

        errorBar.classList.remove('visible');
        errorBar.textContent = '';
      } catch (e) {
        errorBar.textContent = 'Error: ' + e.message;
        errorBar.classList.add('visible');
      }
    }

    function scheduleCompile() {
      clearTimeout(compileTimer);
      compileTimer = setTimeout(compileAndRender, 300);
    }

    editor.addEventListener('input', scheduleCompile);

    // ─── Tab support ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    editor.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Tab') {
        e.preventDefault();
        const start = this.selectionStart;
        const end = this.selectionEnd;
        this.value = this.value.substring(0, start) + '    ' + this.value.substring(end);
        this.selectionStart = this.selectionEnd = start + 4;
        scheduleCompile();
      }
    });

    // ─── Example Switching ──────────────────────────────────────────────

    exampleSelect.addEventListener('change', function() {
      const key = this.value;
      if (EXAMPLES[key]) {
        editor.value = EXAMPLES[key];
        compileAndRender();
      }
    });

    // ─── Copy HTML ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    document.getElementById('btnCopy').addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (!lastCompiledHtml) return;
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(lastCompiledHtml).then(function() {
        showToast('HTML copied to clipboard');
      }).catch(function() {
        // Fallback
        const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
        ta.value = lastCompiledHtml;
        document.body.appendChild(ta);
        ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
        document.body.removeChild(ta);
        showToast('HTML copied to clipboard');
      });
    });

    // ─── Download HTML ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    document.getElementById('btnDownload').addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (!lastCompiledHtml) return;
      const blob = new Blob([lastCompiledHtml], { type: 'text/html' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = (exampleSelect.value || 'ncui-output') + '.html';
      a.click();
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      showToast('File downloaded');
    });

    // ─── Toast ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    function showToast(msg) {
      toast.textContent = msg;
      toast.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.remove('show'); }, 2000);
    }

    // ─── Resize Handle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    (function() {
      const handle = document.getElementById('resizeHandle');
      const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editorPanel');
      let isResizing = false;

      handle.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
        isResizing = true;
        handle.classList.add('active');
        document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
        document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        e.preventDefault();
      });

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
        if (!isResizing) return;
        const containerWidth = document.querySelector('.main').offsetWidth;
        const newWidth = Math.max(250, Math.min(e.clientX, containerWidth - 250));
        editorPanel.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
        if (isResizing) {
          isResizing = false;
          handle.classList.remove('active');
          document.body.style.cursor = '';
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
      });
    })();

    // ─── Init ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    editor.value = EXAMPLES.portfolio;
    compileAndRender();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

    // Floating particles
    (function() {
      var colors = ['0, 212, 255', '124, 58, 237', '255, 107, 203'];
      for (var i = 0; i < 12; i++) {
        var p = document.createElement('div');
        p.className = 'particle';
        var size = Math.random() * 4 + 2;
        p.style.width = size + 'px';
        p.style.height = size + 'px';
        p.style.left = Math.random() * 100 + '%';
        p.style.bottom = '-10px';
        p.style.background = 'rgba(' + colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)] + ', 0.4)';
        p.style.animationDuration = (Math.random() * 10 + 8) + 's';
        p.style.animationDelay = (Math.random() * 10) + 's';
        document.body.appendChild(p);
      }
    })();
  </script>

          <div class="step-number">2</div>

          <span class="step-arrow">&#8594;</span>
        </div>
        <div class="step reveal reveal-delay-3">
          <div class="step-number">3</div>

  <script>
    /* ─── Scroll-triggered reveals ────────────────────────── */
    (function() {
      var reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
      var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
        entries.forEach(function(entry) {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            entry.target.classList.add('visible');
          }
        });
      }, { threshold: 0.1, rootMargin: '0px 0px -40px 0px' });
      reveals.forEach(function(el) { observer.observe(el); });
    })();

    /* ─── Nav scroll effect ───────────────────────────────── */
    (function() {
      var nav = document.getElementById('nav');
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
        if (window.scrollY > 60) {
          nav.classList.add('scrolled');
        } else {
          nav.classList.remove('scrolled');
        }
      });
    })();

    /* ─── Mobile menu ─────────────────────────────────────── */
    var mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobileMenu');
    document.getElementById('mobileToggle').addEventListener('click', function() {
      mobileMenu.classList.add('open');
    });
    document.getElementById('mobileClose').addEventListener('click', function() {
      mobileMenu.classList.remove('open');
    });
    function closeMobile() {
      mobileMenu.classList.remove('open');
    }

    /* ─── Particle / Glow Canvas ──────────────────────────── */
    (function() {
      var canvas = document.getElementById('particles');
      var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      var particles = [];
      var particleCount = 40;

      function resize() {
        canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
        canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
      }
      resize();
      window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

      function Particle() {
        this.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;
        this.y = Math.random() * canvas.height;
        this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3;
        this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3;
        this.radius = Math.random() * 1.5 + 0.5;
        this.opacity = Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.05;
        this.color = Math.random() > 0.5 ? '0, 212, 255' : '124, 58, 237';
      }

      for (var i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
        particles.push(new Particle());
      }

      function animate() {
        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        particles.forEach(function(p) {
          p.x += p.vx;
          p.y += p.vy;
          if (p.x < 0 || p.x > canvas.width) p.vx *= -1;
          if (p.y < 0 || p.y > canvas.height) p.vy *= -1;
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(' + p.color + ',' + p.opacity + ')';
          ctx.fill();
        });

        // Draw connections
        for (var i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
          for (var j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
            var dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
            var dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
            var dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
            if (dist < 150) {
              ctx.beginPath();
              ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
              ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
              ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,' + (0.03 * (1 - dist / 150)) + ')';
              ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
              ctx.stroke();
            }
          }
        }

        requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      }
      animate();
    })();
  </script>
</body>

  <script>
    // ─── Examples ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    const EXAMPLES = {
      portfolio: `page "John Doe — Portfolio"
theme "dark"
accent "#00d4ff"

    brand "JD"

    // ─── DOM ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    const editor = document.getElementById('editor');
    const preview = document.getElementById('preview');
    const errorBar = document.getElementById('errorBar');
    const lineCount = document.getElementById('lineCount');
    const compileTime = document.getElementById('compileTime');
    const exampleSelect = document.getElementById('exampleSelect');
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');

    // ─── Compile ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    let compileTimer = null;
    let lastCompiledHtml = '';

    function compileAndRender() {
      const source = editor.value;
      const lines = source.split('\n').length;
      lineCount.textContent = lines + ' line' + (lines === 1 ? '' : 's');

      try {
        const start = performance.now();
        const html = NCUI.compile(source);
        const elapsed = (performance.now() - start).toFixed(1);
        compileTime.textContent = elapsed + 'ms';

        lastCompiledHtml = html;

        const doc = preview.contentDocument || preview.contentWindow.document;
        doc.open();
        doc.write(html);
        doc.close();

        errorBar.classList.remove('visible');
        errorBar.textContent = '';
      } catch (e) {
        errorBar.textContent = 'Error: ' + e.message;
        errorBar.classList.add('visible');
      }
    }

    function scheduleCompile() {
      clearTimeout(compileTimer);
      compileTimer = setTimeout(compileAndRender, 300);
    }

    editor.addEventListener('input', scheduleCompile);

    // ─── Tab support ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    editor.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Tab') {
        e.preventDefault();
        const start = this.selectionStart;
        const end = this.selectionEnd;
        this.value = this.value.substring(0, start) + '    ' + this.value.substring(end);
        this.selectionStart = this.selectionEnd = start + 4;
        scheduleCompile();
      }
    });

    // ─── Example Switching ──────────────────────────────────────────────

    exampleSelect.addEventListener('change', function() {
      const key = this.value;
      if (EXAMPLES[key]) {
        editor.value = EXAMPLES[key];
        compileAndRender();
      }
    });

    // ─── Copy HTML ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    document.getElementById('btnCopy').addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (!lastCompiledHtml) return;
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(lastCompiledHtml).then(function() {
        showToast('HTML copied to clipboard');
      }).catch(function() {
        // Fallback
        const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
        ta.value = lastCompiledHtml;
        document.body.appendChild(ta);
        ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
        document.body.removeChild(ta);
        showToast('HTML copied to clipboard');
      });
    });

    // ─── Download HTML ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    document.getElementById('btnDownload').addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (!lastCompiledHtml) return;
      const blob = new Blob([lastCompiledHtml], { type: 'text/html' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = (exampleSelect.value || 'ncui-output') + '.html';
      a.click();
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      showToast('File downloaded');
    });

    // ─── Toast ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    function showToast(msg) {
      toast.textContent = msg;
      toast.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.remove('show'); }, 2000);
    }

    // ─── Resize Handle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    (function() {
      const handle = document.getElementById('resizeHandle');
      const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editorPanel');
      let isResizing = false;

      handle.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
        isResizing = true;
        handle.classList.add('active');
        document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
        document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        e.preventDefault();
      });

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
        if (!isResizing) return;
        const containerWidth = document.querySelector('.main').offsetWidth;
        const newWidth = Math.max(250, Math.min(e.clientX, containerWidth - 250));
        editorPanel.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
        if (isResizing) {
          isResizing = false;
          handle.classList.remove('active');
          document.body.style.cursor = '';
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
      });
    })();

    // ─── Init ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    editor.value = EXAMPLES.portfolio;
    compileAndRender();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

<!-- Built with NC -->
<section class="nc-section" id="nc">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-label">Technology</div>
    <h2 class="section-title">Built with NC</h2>
    <p class="section-sub">NeuralEdge is built entirely in NC &mdash; a systems programming language designed for performance, safety, and AI-native development.</p>

    <div class="nc-highlight">
      <div>
        <div class="nc-code">
          <div class="nc-code-header">
            <span>neuraledge/analysis/rsi.nc</span>
            <span style="color:var(--gold)">NC</span>
          </div>
          <pre><span class="cm">// RSI calculation with configurable period</span>
<span class="kw">fn</span> <span class="fn">calculate_rsi</span>(prices: <span class="kw">Vec</span>&lt;<span class="kw">f64</span>&gt;, period: <span class="kw">u32</span>) -&gt; <span class="kw">f64</span> {
    <span class="kw">let</span> changes = <span class="fn">price_deltas</span>(prices);
    <span class="kw">let</span> gains = <span class="fn">filter_positive</span>(changes);
    <span class="kw">let</span> losses = <span class="fn">filter_negative</span>(changes);

    <span class="kw">let</span> avg_gain = <span class="fn">ema</span>(gains, period);
    <span class="kw">let</span> avg_loss = <span class="fn">ema</span>(losses, period);

    <span class="kw">let</span> rs = avg_gain / avg_loss;
    <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="str">100.0</span> - (<span class="str">100.0</span> / (<span class="str">1.0</span> + rs));
}

<span class="cm">// Self-learning prediction feedback loop</span>
<span class="kw">fn</span> <span class="fn">update_model</span>(prediction: <span class="kw">Signal</span>, actual: <span class="kw">f64</span>) {
    <span class="kw">let</span> accuracy = <span class="fn">measure_accuracy</span>(prediction, actual);
    <span class="fn">adjust_weights</span>(accuracy);
    <span class="fn">log_performance</span>(<span class="str">"model_v2"</span>, accuracy);
}</pre>
        </div>

        <div class="nc-stats">
          <div class="nc-stat">
            <div class="val">21,000+</div>
            <div class="lbl">Lines of NC Code</div>
          </div>
          <div class="nc-stat">
            <div class="val">100%</div>
            <div class="lbl">Pure NC</div>
          </div>
          <div class="nc-stat">
            <div class="val">81+</div>
            <div class="lbl">API Endpoints</div>
          </div>
          <div class="nc-stat">
            <div class="val">30+</div>
            <div class="lbl">Indicators</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h3 style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:16px">Why NC?</h3>
        <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:20px">
          <div>
            <h4 style="font-size:1rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gold);margin-bottom:4px">Systems-Level Performance</h4>
            <p style="font-size:.9rem;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.6">NC delivers C-level performance with modern safety guarantees. Every microsecond matters when processing real-time market data.</p>
          </div>
          <div>
            <h4 style="font-size:1rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gold);margin-bottom:4px">AI-Native Design</h4>
            <p style="font-size:.9rem;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.6">Built from the ground up with AI workflows in mind. NC's type system and concurrency model make building intelligent systems natural.</p>
          </div>
          <div>
            <h4 style="font-size:1rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gold);margin-bottom:4px">Memory Safety</h4>
            <p style="font-size:.9rem;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.6">No buffer overflows, no use-after-free. Financial systems demand reliability, and NC delivers it at the language level.</p>
          </div>
          <div>
            <h4 style="font-size:1rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gold);margin-bottom:4px">Expressive Syntax</h4>
            <p style="font-size:.9rem;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.6">21,000+ lines that are readable and maintainable. NC's clean syntax keeps complex financial logic comprehensible.</p>

      </div>
      <div class="step">
        <div class="step-num">3</div>
        <div class="step-content">

      </div>

    <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--dim);margin-left:8px">by <a href="https://devheallabs.in" target="_blank" style="color:var(--accent2);text-decoration:none">DevHeal Labs AI</a></span>

<script>
var API=location.protocol==='file:'?'http://localhost:9090':'';

function showTab(name,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('active')});
  if(el)el.classList.add('active');
  if(name==='investigate')renderInvestigate();
  if(name==='k8s')renderK8s();
  if(name==='knowledge')renderKnowledge();
  if(name==='validate')renderValidate();
}

function renderInvestigate(){
  document.getElementById('content').innerHTML=
    '<div class="section-title"><span class="icon">&#128269;</span> Investigate Incident</div>'+
    '<div class="card"><div class="card-header"><span class="icon">&#128203;</span> Incident Data</div><div class="card-body">'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Service Name</label><input class="input" id="iSvc" placeholder="e.g. checkout-api, payments-svc"></div>'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Description</label><input class="input" id="iDesc" placeholder="e.g. HTTP 500 errors since 15:42 UTC"></div>'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Logs</label><textarea class="input" id="iLogs" rows="3" placeholder="Paste log entries..."></textarea></div>'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Metrics</label><textarea class="input" id="iMetrics" rows="2" placeholder="Paste metrics data..."></textarea></div>'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Errors</label><textarea class="input" id="iErrors" rows="2" placeholder="Paste error messages..."></textarea></div>'+
    '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Deploy History</label><textarea class="input" id="iDeploys" rows="2" placeholder="Recent deployments..."></textarea></div>'+
    '<div class="btn-row">'+
    '<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="doInvestigate()">&#9889; Investigate with AI</button>'+
    '<button class="btn btn-success" onclick="loadSample()">&#128230; Load Sample</button>'+
    '<button class="btn" onclick="doQuickAnalyze()">&#9889; Quick Analyze</button>'+
    '</div></div></div>'+
    '<div id="iResult"></div>';
}

function loadSample(){
  apiFetch('/sample',{}).then(function(d){
    document.getElementById('iSvc').value=d.service_name||'';
    document.getElementById('iDesc').value=d.description||'';
    document.getElementById('iLogs').value=d.logs||'';
    document.getElementById('iMetrics').value=d.metrics||'';
    document.getElementById('iErrors').value=d.errors||'';
    document.getElementById('iDeploys').value=d.deploy_history||'';
  });
}

function doInvestigate(){
  var body={service_name:gv('iSvc'),description:gv('iDesc'),logs:gv('iLogs'),metrics:gv('iMetrics'),errors:gv('iErrors'),deploy_history:gv('iDeploys')};
  document.getElementById('iResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-body" style="text-align:center;padding:40px"><div class="loader"></div> 4 AI agents analyzing your data... (15-30s)</div></div>';
  apiFetch('/investigate/manual',body,'POST').then(function(d){renderReport(d,'iResult');}).catch(showErr('iResult'));
}

function doQuickAnalyze(){
  var text=gv('iLogs')+'\n'+gv('iMetrics')+'\n'+gv('iErrors');
  document.getElementById('iResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-body" style="text-align:center;padding:30px"><div class="loader"></div> Analyzing...</div></div>';
  apiFetch('/analyze',{text:text,context:gv('iSvc')},'POST').then(function(d){
    var h='<div class="card"><div class="card-header" style="color:var(--red)"><span class="icon">&#9888;</span> Quick Analysis</div><div class="card-body">';
    h+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:12px;margin-bottom:16px">';
    h+='<div class="report-metric"><div class="value" style="color:var(--accent2)">'+(d.confidence_percent||0)+'%</div><div class="label">Confidence</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="report-metric"><div><span class="badge badge-'+(d.severity==='critical'?'red':d.severity==='high'?'amber':'blue')+'">'+(d.severity||'?')+'</span></div><div class="label">Severity</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="report-metric"><div><span class="badge badge-blue">'+(d.category||'?')+'</span></div><div class="label">Category</div></div>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:12px 16px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);border-left:3px solid var(--red);margin-bottom:12px"><strong>Root Cause:</strong> '+esc(d.root_cause||'?')+'</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:12px 16px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);border-left:3px solid var(--green);margin-bottom:12px"><strong>Fix:</strong> '+esc(d.immediate_action||'?')+'</div>';
    if(d.command)h+='<div class="fix-cmd" onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.textContent)">'+esc(d.command)+'</div>';
    h+='</div></div>';
    document.getElementById('iResult').innerHTML=h;
  }).catch(showErr('iResult'));
}

    '<div class="section-title"><span class="icon">&#9781;</span> Kubernetes</div>'+

    '<div class="btn-row">'+

function k8sUnhealthy(){setLoading('kResult');apiFetch('/k8s/unhealthy').then(function(d){document.getElementById('kResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">&#128308; Unhealthy Pods</div><div class="card-body"><div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div></div></div>';}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}
function k8sEvents(){setLoading('kResult');apiFetch('/k8s/events',{namespace:''},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('kResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">&#128196; Events</div><div class="card-body"><div class="result-box">'+esc(typeof d.events==='string'?d.events:JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div></div></div>';}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}
function k8sLogs(){apiFetch('/k8s/logs',{pod_name:gv('kPod'),namespace:gv('kNs'),lines:50},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('kResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">Logs: '+esc(gv('kPod'))+'</div><div class="card-body"><div class="result-box">'+esc(typeof d.logs==='string'?d.logs:JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div></div></div>';}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}
function k8sRestart(){apiFetch('/k8s/fix',{action:'restart',target:gv('kPod'),namespace:gv('kNs'),secret:''},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('kResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}
function k8sRollback(){apiFetch('/k8s/fix',{action:'rollback',target:gv('kPod'),namespace:gv('kNs'),secret:''},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('kResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}
function k8sInvestigate(){setLoading('kResult','AI investigating namespace...');apiFetch('/k8s/investigate',{namespace:gv('kInvNs'),description:gv('kInvDesc')},'POST').then(function(d){renderReport(d.diagnosis||d,'kResult');}).catch(showErr('kResult'));}

function loadKnowledge(){setLoading('knResult');apiFetch('/knowledge').then(function(d){document.getElementById('knResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">&#128161; Knowledge</div><div class="card-body"><div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div></div></div>';}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}
function loadIncidents(){apiFetch('/incidents').then(function(d){var h='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">&#128203; Past Incidents ('+(d.incidents||[]).length+')</div><div class="card-body">';if((d.incidents||[]).length===0)h+='<div style="color:var(--dim);text-align:center;padding:20px">No incidents yet. Run an investigation first.</div>';(d.incidents||[]).forEach(function(id){h+='<div style="padding:8px 12px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:6px;margin:4px 0;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px" onclick="viewIncident(\''+id+'\')"><span class="badge badge-blue">'+id+'</span><span style="color:var(--dim);font-size:12px">Click to view</span></div>';});h+='</div></div>';document.getElementById('knResult').innerHTML=h;}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}
function viewIncident(id){apiFetch('/incident',{incident_id:id},'POST').then(function(d){renderReport(d,'knResult');}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}
function indexDocs(){apiFetch('/rag/index').then(function(d){document.getElementById('knResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}
function ragSearch(){apiFetch('/rag/search',{query:gv('ragQ')},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('knResult').innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-header">&#128270; Results</div><div class="card-body"><div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div></div></div>';}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}
function giveFeedback(){apiFetch('/feedback',{incident_id:gv('fbId'),correct:gv('fbCorrect'),notes:gv('fbNotes')},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('knResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('knResult'));}

function checkHealth(){apiFetch('/health').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function checkConfig(){apiFetch('/config').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function checkMcp(){apiFetch('/mcp/tools').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function checkMonitor(){apiFetch('/monitor',{},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function triggerWatchdog(){apiFetch('/watchdog',{},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function selfHeal(auto){setLoading('vResult','Self-healing...');apiFetch('/self-heal',{service_name:gv('shSvc'),description:gv('shDesc'),auto_execute:auto,secret:gv('shSecret')},'POST').then(function(d){renderReport(d,'vResult');}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}
function nnClassify(){apiFetch('/nn/classify',{error_rate:+gv('nnErr'),latency_ms:+gv('nnLat'),cpu_percent:+gv('nnCpu'),memory_percent:+gv('nnMem'),recent_deploy:+gv('nnDep')},'POST').then(function(d){document.getElementById('vResult').innerHTML='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';}).catch(showErr('vResult'));}

function sendChat(){
  var msg=document.getElementById('chatIn').value.trim();if(!msg)return;
  document.getElementById('chatIn').value='';
  addChat(msg,'user');
  addChat('<div class="loader"></div> Thinking...','bot',true);
  apiFetch('/chat',{message:msg,session_id:'ui'},'POST').then(function(d){
    removeLast();
    var reply=d.reply||d.content||d.response||d;
    if(typeof reply==='object')reply=reply.response||reply.content||reply.reply||JSON.stringify(reply);
    if(typeof reply==='string'){
      reply=reply.replace(/^```json\s*/,'').replace(/```\s*$/,'').trim();
      try{var p=JSON.parse(reply);reply=p.response||p.content||p.reply||p.message||reply;}catch(e){}
    }
    addChat(reply,'bot');
  }).catch(function(e){removeLast();addChat('Error: '+e.message,'bot');});
}
function addChat(msg,role,isHtml){
  var el=document.getElementById('chatMsgs');
  var d=document.createElement('div');d.className='chat-bubble '+role;
  if(isHtml)d.innerHTML=msg;else d.textContent=msg;
  el.appendChild(d);el.scrollTop=el.scrollHeight;
}
function removeLast(){var el=document.getElementById('chatMsgs');if(el.lastChild)el.removeChild(el.lastChild);}

function renderReport(d,targetId){
  var h='';
  if(d.root_cause){
    h+='<div class="card"><div class="card-header" style="color:var(--red)"><span class="icon">&#9888;</span> '+(d.incident_id||'Analysis Report')+'</div><div class="card-body">';
    h+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:16px;margin-bottom:20px">';
    h+='<div class="report-metric"><div class="value" style="color:'+(((d.confidence||d.confidence_percent||0)>70)?'var(--green)':'var(--amber)')+'">'+(d.confidence||d.confidence_percent||0)+'%</div><div class="label">Confidence</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="report-metric"><div><span class="badge badge-red">'+(d.category||'?')+'</span></div><div class="label">Category</div></div>';
    if(d.signals_total)h+='<div class="report-metric"><div class="value" style="color:var(--amber)">'+d.signals_total+'</div><div class="label">Signals</div></div>';
    else h+='<div class="report-metric"><div><span class="badge badge-'+(d.severity==='critical'?'red':'amber')+'">'+(d.severity||'?')+'</span></div><div class="label">Severity</div></div>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:14px 18px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);border-left:4px solid var(--red);margin-bottom:16px;font-size:14px"><strong>Root Cause:</strong> '+esc(d.root_cause)+'</div>';
    if(d.affected_services&&d.affected_services.length)h+='<div style="margin-bottom:12px"><strong>Affected Services:</strong> '+d.affected_services.map(function(s){return '<span class="badge badge-blue">'+esc(s)+'</span>';}).join(' ')+'</div>';
    h+='</div></div>';
  }
  if(d.evidence_chain&&d.evidence_chain.length){
    h+='<div class="card"><div class="card-header"><span class="icon">&#128270;</span> Evidence ('+d.evidence_chain.length+')</div><div class="card-body">';
    d.evidence_chain.forEach(function(e){h+='<div class="evidence-item">'+esc(e)+'</div>';});
    h+='</div></div>';
  }
  if(d.timeline&&d.timeline.length){
    h+='<div class="card"><div class="card-header"><span class="icon">&#128337;</span> Timeline</div><div class="card-body">';
    d.timeline.forEach(function(t){h+='<div class="timeline-item"><span class="time">'+esc(t.time)+'</span><span>'+esc(t.event)+'</span></div>';});
    h+='</div></div>';
  }
  if(d.remediation||d.immediate_actions){
    var rem=d.remediation||d;
    h+='<div class="card"><div class="card-header" style="color:var(--green)"><span class="icon">&#128295;</span> Remediation</div><div class="card-body">';
    (rem.immediate_actions||[]).forEach(function(a){
      h+='<div class="fix-step"><span class="step-num">Step '+(a.step||0)+'</span> — '+esc(a.action||a.description||'');
      if(a.command)h+='<div class="fix-cmd" onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.textContent)">'+esc(a.command)+'</div>';
      if(a.risk)h+=' <span class="badge badge-'+(a.risk==='high'?'red':a.risk==='medium'?'amber':'green')+'">'+a.risk+' risk</span>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
    if(rem.verification){h+='<div style="margin-top:12px"><strong>Verify:</strong></div>';rem.verification.forEach(function(v){h+='<div style="padding:4px 0;font-size:12px;color:var(--green)">&#10003; '+esc(v)+'</div>';});}
    h+='</div></div>';
  }
  if(!h)h='<div class="result-box">'+esc(JSON.stringify(d,null,2))+'</div>';
  document.getElementById(targetId).innerHTML=h;
}

function gv(id){return(document.getElementById(id)||{}).value||'';}
function esc(s){var d=document.createElement('div');d.textContent=s||'';return d.innerHTML;}
function showErr(id){return function(e){document.getElementById(id).innerHTML='<div class="result-box error">Error: '+esc(e.message)+'</div>';};}
function setLoading(id,msg){document.getElementById(id).innerHTML='<div class="card"><div class="card-body" style="text-align:center;padding:40px"><div class="loader"></div> '+(msg||'Loading...')+'</div></div>';}
function apiFetch(path,body,method){
  var opts={headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}};
  if(method==='POST'||body){opts.method='POST';opts.body=JSON.stringify(body||{});}
  return fetch(API+path,opts).then(function(r){return r.json();}).then(function(d){return d.data?JSON.parse(d.data):d;});
}

renderInvestigate();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!-- Features -->
<section id="features">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header">
      <p class="section-label">Features</p>
      <h2 class="section-title">Everything You Need for Autonomous Ops</h2>
      <p class="section-subtitle">From detection to remediation, SwarmOps covers the full incident lifecycle with specialized AI agents.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="features-grid">
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon green">&#9889;</div>
        <h3>Real-Time Incident Detection</h3>
        <p>Continuously monitors Prometheus metrics and Elasticsearch logs to detect anomalies the moment they surface. Configurable thresholds and pattern matching.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon cyan">&#128269;</div>
        <h3>AI-Driven Root Cause Analysis</h3>
        <p>Investigation agents correlate signals across metrics, logs, and traces to pinpoint the root cause. Reduces MTTR from hours to minutes.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon green">&#9881;</div>
        <h3>Automated Remediation</h3>
        <p>Kubernetes-native remediation: pod restarts, scaling, rollbacks, and config patches executed automatically with safety guardrails.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon cyan">&#129504;</div>
        <h3>Reinforcement Learning</h3>
        <p>Q-value updates for action selection let SwarmOps learn which remediation strategies work best for each incident type over time.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon green">&#128218;</div>
        <h3>RAG Knowledge Base</h3>
        <p>Retrieval-Augmented Generation connects agents to your runbooks, past incidents, and documentation for context-aware decision making.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon cyan">&#128736;</div>
        <h3>GitHub Integration</h3>
        <p>Automatically creates pull requests with fixes, links issues to incidents, and tracks remediation through your existing Git workflow.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="feature-card">
        <div class="feature-icon green">&#128214;</div>
        <h3>Runbook Automation</h3>
        <p>Encode your operations knowledge as executable runbooks. SwarmOps agents select and execute the right runbook for each incident class.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- How It Works -->
<section id="how-it-works">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header">
      <p class="section-label">How It Works</p>
      <h2 class="section-title">The SwarmOps Pipeline</h2>
      <p class="section-subtitle">Five stages from signal to resolution, powered by collaborating AI agents.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="pipeline">
      <div class="pipeline-step">
        <div class="step-circle">&#128225;</div>
        <h4>Monitor</h4>
        <p>Ingest metrics and logs from Prometheus &amp; Elasticsearch in real time</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pipeline-step">
        <div class="step-circle">&#128680;</div>
        <h4>Detect</h4>
        <p>Anomaly detection agents identify incidents using configurable rules &amp; ML</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pipeline-step">
        <div class="step-circle">&#128270;</div>
        <h4>Investigate</h4>
        <p>Root cause analysis correlates signals, queries the RAG knowledge base</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pipeline-step">
        <div class="step-circle">&#9889;</div>
        <h4>Remediate</h4>
        <p>Execute automated fixes via Kubernetes, GitHub PRs, or runbooks</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pipeline-step">
        <div class="step-circle">&#127891;</div>
        <h4>Learn</h4>
        <p>RL agent updates Q-values to improve future action selection</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- Integrations -->
<section id="integrations">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header">
      <p class="section-label">Integrations</p>
      <h2 class="section-title">Connects to Your Stack</h2>
      <p class="section-subtitle">Native integrations with the tools you already run in production.</p>

    <div class="integrations-grid">
      <div class="integration-card">
