      </div>
      <div class="integration-card">
        <div class="integration-icon">&#128269;</div>
        <h4>Elasticsearch</h4>
        <p>Query logs at scale. Pattern matching and anomaly detection across structured and unstructured data.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="integration-card">
        <div class="integration-icon">&#9784;</div>
        <h4>Kubernetes</h4>
        <p>Full cluster access for remediation: pod management, scaling, rollbacks, and config updates.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="integration-card">
        <div class="integration-icon">
          <svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M12 0C5.37 0 0 5.37 0 12c0 5.31 3.435 9.795 8.205 11.385.6.105.825-.255.825-.57 0-.285-.015-1.23-.015-2.235-3.015.555-3.795-.735-4.035-1.41-.135-.345-.72-1.41-1.23-1.695-.42-.225-1.02-.78-.015-.795.945-.015 1.62.87 1.845 1.23 1.08 1.815 2.805 1.305 3.495.99.105-.78.42-1.305.765-1.605-2.67-.3-5.46-1.335-5.46-5.925 0-1.305.465-2.385 1.23-3.225-.12-.3-.54-1.53.12-3.18 0 0 1.005-.315 3.3 1.23.96-.27 1.98-.405 3-.405s2.04.135 3 .405c2.295-1.56 3.3-1.23 3.3-1.23.66 1.65.24 2.88.12 3.18.765.84 1.23 1.905 1.23 3.225 0 4.605-2.805 5.625-5.475 5.925.435.375.81 1.095.81 2.22 0 1.605-.015 2.895-.015 3.3 0 .315.225.69.825.57A12.02 12.02 0 0024 12c0-6.63-5.37-12-12-12z"/></svg>
        </div>
        <h4>GitHub</h4>
        <p>Automated PRs, issue linking, and commit-level traceability for every remediation action.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- Built with NC -->
<section id="nc">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="nc-section">
      <div>
        <p class="section-label">Core Technology</p>
        <h2>Built with NC</h2>
        <p>SwarmOps is powered by the NC programming language &mdash; a systems language designed for middleware, networking, and high-performance agent orchestration.</p>
        <ul class="nc-features">
          <li>High-performance middleware execution</li>
          <li>Native agent lifecycle management</li>
          <li>Built-in observability and logging</li>
          <li>Lightweight deployment engine</li>
          <li>Extensible with C-level performance</li>
        </ul>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-code">
        <span class="cmt">// SwarmOps detection agent in NC</span><br>
        <span class="kw">agent</span> <span class="fn">detection_agent</span> {<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="kw">source</span>: <span class="str">"prometheus"</span>,<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="kw">threshold</span>: <span class="str">0.95</span>,<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="kw">on_alert</span>: <span class="fn">investigate</span>,<br>
        }<br><br>
        <span class="kw">fn</span> <span class="fn">investigate</span>(incident) {<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="kw">let</span> context = <span class="fn">rag_query</span>(incident.signal)<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="kw">let</span> action = <span class="fn">q_select</span>(incident, context)<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="fn">remediate</span>(action)<br>
        &nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="fn">learn</span>(incident, action, action.reward)<br>
        }
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- Quick Start -->
<section id="quickstart">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="section-header">
      <p class="section-label">Quick Start</p>
      <h2 class="section-title">Up and Running in Minutes</h2>
      <p class="section-subtitle">Three steps to deploy SwarmOps in your environment.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="quickstart-steps">
      <div class="qs-step">
        <div class="qs-num">1</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Clone and Install</h4>
          <code>git clone https://github.com/nicobench/swarmops.git<br>cd swarmops &amp;&amp; make install</code>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="qs-step">
        <div class="qs-num">2</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Configure Your Environment</h4>
          <code>cp config/example.nc config/production.nc<br># Edit production.nc with your Prometheus, K8s, and GitHub endpoints</code>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="qs-step">
        <div class="qs-num">3</div>
        <div>
          <h4>Launch SwarmOps</h4>
          <code>swarmops start --config config/production.nc</code>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>
